## рҹ‘‘ v3.92.0 вҖ” *"Comfort"* вҖ” keyboard hotkeys & reaction toggle (Pillar 2: QoL)

> Two more comforts BG3 players never think about until they're gone.

- вҢЁпёҸ **Keyboard hotkeys** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” `1`-`9` arm the matching ability (now numbered
  on the buttons), `V` shove, `X` disengage, `U` undo, `Enter` end turn, `F` forecast, `R` reactions.
  Pure `hotkey()` map, headless-safe listener.
- вҡЎ **Reaction toggle** вҖ” a button (BG3's "ask before my opportunity attacks"): flip it off and your
  heroes won't spend their reaction on opportunity attacks. Enemies still do.
- рҹ§Ә `qol.test.js` extended (now **17 checks**): the full hotkey map + the reaction-toggle wiring,
  on top of the Undo predicate. Smoke still **400 games, 0 errors**. Headless suite now **338 checks**,
  all green.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.91.0 вҖ” *"Take It Back"* вҖ” Undo Move (Pillar 2: Quality of Life begins)

> The first comfort BG3 players lean on constantly. No more fat-fingered, turn-ruining clicks.

- вҶ© **Undo Move** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” a new action: take back the active hero's move and
  get the movement **refunded**, as long as the move **triggered nothing irreversible** (no surface
  effect applied, no opportunity attack provoked, and you survived). If a step into fire or out of a
  foe's reach happened, the move is *committed* (BG3-honest) and Undo greys out.
- рҹ§Ә **`qol.test.js`** lifts the page's real `canUndoMove` predicate and proves a clean move is
  undoable while a dirty/lethal one isn't, plus the wiring (snapshot, dirtied-by-surface/OA, restore,
  cleared on act/turn) вҖ” 10 checks. Smoke still **400 games, 0 errors**. Headless suite now **331
  checks**, all green.
- рҹҺҜ First **Pillar 2 (Quality of Life)** entry on [the BG3 roadmap](docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md).

## рҹ‘‘ v3.90.0 вҖ” *"No Free Retreat"* вҖ” opportunity attacks & Disengage (Pillar 1 continues)

> Positioning gets teeth: you can't just walk away from a foe anymore.

- вҡ”пёҸ **Opportunity attacks** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” moving **out of an adjacent foe's reach**
  provokes a **free melee strike** from that foe (once per round, for *both* sides вҖ” enemies provoke
  when fleeing too). Fully reprojected into the iso board with the lunge animation + combat log.
- рҹҸғ **Disengage** вҖ” a new action: spend it and your movement this turn **draws no opportunity
  attacks** (the tactical-retreat option). Reaction state resets at the start of each unit's turn.
- рҹ§Ә **`opportunity.test.js`** lifts the page's real reach-test and proves OAs fire **only when
  leaving reach** (not when staying, shuffling, approaching, or passing by), plus the wiring
  (Disengage, once-per-round, turn reset) вҖ” 11 checks. Smoke still auto-plays **400 games, 0 errors**,
  balance intact. Headless suite now **321 checks**, all green.
- рҹҺҜ `docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md` вҖ” opportunity attacks marked shipped.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.89.0 вҖ” *"The High Ground"* вҖ” height advantage (Pillar 1 continues)

> "I have the high ground." Now it actually matters.

- вӣ°пёҸ **Height advantage** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” a contested **raised mound** in the middle of
  the arena. Striking from **higher ground grants advantage**; striking from **below, disadvantage**.
  Folded consistently into the hit math (`resolve`), the XCOM-style **forecast**, and the incoming-
  **threat** readout вҖ” so the % you see already reflects the ground you're standing on. High tiles
  are gilded with a в–І marker, units **stand taller** on them, and the Selected panel flags *в–І high
  ground*.
- рҹ§Ә **`height.test.js`** lifts the page's real elevation helpers and proves highвҶ’advantage,
  lowвҶ’disadvantage, levelвҶ’neither, plus the wiring into hit math / forecast / view (9 checks). Smoke
  still auto-plays **400 games, 0 errors**, balance intact. Headless suite now **310 checks**, all green.
- рҹҺҜ `docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md` вҖ” height advantage marked shipped.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.88.0 вҖ” *"Storm & Tide"* вҖ” electrified water (Pillar 1 continues)

> The other combo every BG3 player learns: **water + lightning**. Soak them, then shock them.

- вҡЎ **Electrified water** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” Garrow's new **Hallowed Water** conjures a
  water surface (and douses fire); Varra's new **Storm Bolt** (lightning) **arcs through any water**
  and zaps *everyone* standing in it for bonus damage + Slowed. A two-hero combo: soak the cluster,
  then shock it.
- рҹ§Ә `surfaces.test.js` extended (now **13 checks**): `isWaterAt` detection + the full lightning/water
  wiring (the `chainWater` ability, `chainLightning`, the `applyOne` trigger). Smoke harness still
  auto-plays **400 games, 0 errors**, balance intact. Headless suite now **301 checks**, all green.
- рҹҺҜ `docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md` вҖ” electrified water marked shipped.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.87.0 вҖ” *"Give Ground"* вҖ” the Shove maneuver (Pillar 1 continues)

> The combo BG3 players reach for first: shove a foe **into your fire**, or **into a wall**.

- рҹ«· **Shove** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” a universal action (its own button): a **Strength
  contest** (attacker STR vs the defender's best of STR/DEX) that pushes the foe **one tile
  directly away**. Push them onto a **hazard surface** and they suffer it (shove-into-fire = the
  BG3 environmental kill); push them into a **wall** and they take impact damage. Pairs directly
  with v3.86.0's surfaces.
- рҹ§Ә **`shove.test.js`** lifts the page's real push-direction helper and proves it pushes a foe
  one tile away in **all 8 directions**, plus that the maneuver is wired (contest, shove-into-
  surface combo, wall impact, the UI button) вҖ” 9 checks. The smoke harness still auto-plays full
  games with zero errors. Headless suite now **299 checks**, all green.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.86.0 вҖ” *"The Battlefield Reacts"* вҖ” environmental surfaces (toward "BG3 but superior")

> The first pillar of the [BG3 roadmap](docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md): BG3's signature combat feature,
> done our way. The ground itself is now a weapon.

- рҹ”Ҙ **Environmental surfaces** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” lay **oil** (Roen's *Oil Flask*),
  then **ignite** it (Garrow's *Firebrand*): fire **spreads** through grease tile-to-tile,
  **burns** anyone standing in it (Burning DoT), and **water douses** it. Surfaces (fire / grease /
  poison / ice / water) apply on enter and at the start of each turn, spread & decay per round,
  and are rendered as animated tiles with their own flickering torch-glow on the iso board.
- рҹ§Ә **`surfaces.test.js`** lifts the page's *real* surface logic and proves the combos:
  greaseвҶ’fire ignition, fire spread, water dousing, decay, and in-bounds safety (11 checks). The
  smoke harness auto-plays **400 full games** through it with zero errors and balance intact.
  Headless suite now **290 checks**, all green.
- рҹҺҜ **`docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md`** вҖ” the honest plan for "similar to BG3 but superior in QoL, plot,
  characters & gameplay mechanics": what we build here vs. what needs Unity/art/budget, shipped
  one verified pillar increment at a time.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.85.0 вҖ” *"In Motion"* вҖ” the figures fight, not just stand

> The isometric board was still a diorama. Now the sprites *move*: they turn to face
> their foe, lunge when they strike, recoil when struck, and breathe at rest.

- рҹӨә **Attack choreography** in `play/crown_combat.html` (procedural, no new frames):
  - **Lunge** вҖ” a striker eases toward its target along the iso vector and back
  - **Recoil** вҖ” the struck figure jolts away from the blow
  - **Facing** вҖ” each sprite flips horizontally to face whoever it's fighting
  - **Idle breathing** вҖ” every living figure has a gentle, phase-offset bob so the board
    is never frozen (a little stronger on the active hero)
- All driven off the existing turn flow + frame clock; the engine, forecasts, conditions,
  VFX and lighting are untouched.
- рҹ§Ә `iso.test.js` now also asserts the choreography is wired (lunge/recoil/facing/breathing);
  the smoke harness still auto-plays full games through the animated `draw()`. Headless suite
  now **279 checks**, all green. Preview + bundle rebuilt.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.84.0 вҖ” *"The Tilt"* вҖ” the playable board goes isometric

> The genre's defining look. The Skirmish stops being top-down and becomes a real
> **isometric crypt** вҖ” diamond grid, raised stone walls, depth-sorted sprites.

- рҹ§ӯ **Isometric renderer** in `play/crown_combat.html` вҖ” a 2:1 diamond projection: floor
  tiles are stone diamonds, **walls are extruded 3-D blocks**, and everything (walls, units,
  props) is **depth-sorted back-to-front** so nearer things correctly occlude. The combat
  logic stays on the square grid untouched; only the view + mouse-picking are reprojected.
- рҹ—ҝ **Environmental props** dress the crypt вҖ” real CC0 feature tiles (a dark altar behind the
  boss, flanking statues, a sealed door) as billboards.
- рҹ©ё **Persistent decals** вҖ” blood/scorch is left on the tile where each combatant falls.
- вңЁ The whole juice layer (projectiles, impacts, slashes, crit bursts, torch lighting,
  death wisps, idle-bob) is reprojected into iso. All rules/forecasts/SFX unchanged.
- рҹ§Ә **`iso.test.js`** lifts the page's real projection math and proves click-picking
  round-trips for **all 140 tiles** (centres + interior samples), that the projection is
  injective and in-bounds вҖ” objective coverage for the one thing a screenshot can't show.
  `cc0_art.test.js` updated; the smoke harness still auto-plays full games through the iso
  `draw()`. Headless suite now **278 checks**, all green. Preview + bundle rebuilt.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.83.0 вҖ” *"The Quickening"* вҖ” the combat comes alive (VFX), real art everywhere

> "PLEASE DO MORE." Done: the fight stops being static. Bolts fly, steel sparks, the
> screen kicks, torches breathe вҖ” and the Bestiary now wears the same real sprites.

- вңЁ **Combat juice** in `play/crown_combat.html` (pure-canvas, no assets, works in the bundle):
  - **Projectiles** streak attacker вҶ’ target for ranged/spell hits, with an **impact burst** on
    arrival; **slash arcs** for melee; **crit bursts** with radial sparks.
  - **Screen shake** on hits, harder on crits and kills; **death wisps** rise from the slain
    (fitting, for the Returned).
  - **Dynamic torch lighting** вҖ” warm pools follow the heroes, cold necrotic glow the Returned,
    with a living **flicker**; the active hero gives a gentle **idle-bob**.
  - Damage-typed colours (fire/cold/radiant/necrotic/forceвҖҰ); every rule, forecast & SFX
    unchanged.
- вҳ  **Bestiary now uses the real monster art** вҖ” `tools/make-compendium.py` matches **35/37 foes**
  to the same DCSS sprites the board uses (keyword map, token fallback for the rest).
- рҹӣЎпёҸ Render path stayed headless-safe (the smoke harness auto-plays full games through the new
  `draw()` every run); `cc0_art.test.js` now gates the VFX/lighting/shake wiring. Suite **270 checks**,
  all green. Preview refreshed (`play/combat_preview.png`), hub + bundle rebuilt.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.81.0 вҖ” *"One File"* вҖ” the whole game in a single portable HTML

> "Can you give me a functioning HTML of all of this, including dialog trees?" вҖ” yes:
> **`play/crown_of_horns.html`**, one self-contained file, no server and no other files.

- рҹ“Ұ **`play/crown_of_horns.html`** (~1.1 MB) вҖ” a tabbed shell that bundles all nine browser
  pages and renders each in an isolated `<iframe srcdoc>` so their scripts/styles never
  collide: **Combat** (the real playable engine), **Dialogue** (every branching tree, Map +
  Walk), **Endings**, **Compendium** (Grimoire/Bestiary/Conditions/Codex/Atlas), **Cast**,
  **Flag Graph**, **Saga Map**, **Save Inspector**, **Analytics**.
- рҹ”— In-bundle cross-links are rewired to switch tabs and carry the deep-link hash вҖ” the Saga
  Map's "рҹ’¬ conversation" chips jump straight to that conversation in the Dialogue tab, etc.
  The bundle is itself deep-linkable: `crown_of_horns.html#dialogue:ilfaeril.quest.resolution`.
- рҹ§° `tools/make-all-in-one.py` regenerates it from the standalone pages (JSON-embedded, lazy
  srcdoc load).
- рҹ§Ә `all_in_one.test.js` (14 checks: all 9 pages embedded & parse, marquee payloads intact,
  shell + rewiring + deep-links wired) added to CI. Headless suite now **263 checks**, all green.
- рҹҸ  Hub gains a prominent button to the single-file build.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.80.0 вҖ” *"Real Steel"* вҖ” actual game art enters the repo

> The art blockade is broken. Dungeon Crawl Stone Soup's **CC0 (public-domain) tileset**
> lives on GitHub вҖ” the one reachable host вҖ” and a licensed, curated slice of it is now
> *in the project as real, reusable game assets.*

- рҹҺЁ **114 CC0 tiles** вҶ’ `Assets/Resources/Art/DCSS/` вҖ” crypt/tomb floors &amp; walls, doors,
  altars, statues, **36 monster sprites mapped to our bestiary archetypes** (Returned wights &amp;
  ghouls, sorrow-wraiths, the Hollow Cantor, Kelemvorite templars, Crown-Wars blade-singers,
  Netherese war-constructs, the Herald of the UnmadeвҖҰ), 6 hero-usable humanoids, and 12 real
  weapon/armour/potion item icons.
- вҡ–пёҸ **Licensing done right** (`tools/fetch-cc0-tiles.py`): DCSS's LICENSE declares the tiles
  CC0; the curated `crawl/tiles` reuse project publishes an unknown-license exclusion list вҖ”
  the fetcher downloads that list and **hard-skips anything on it**, then writes
  `Art/DCSS/LICENSE.md` documenting CC0 + provenance for *every* file (source path table).
- рҹ–јпёҸ **`play/gameplay_v2.png`** (`tools/render-gameplay-v2.py`) вҖ” the Cinderhaunt rebuilt from
  the real tiles: lit crypt, the party, the Choir at a necrotic altar, tactical overlays,
  sprite portraits and real item icons in the HUD. BG1-era fidelity from actual licensed art.
- рҹ§Ә `cc0_art.test.js` (11 checks: PNG magic on every file, group counts, LICENSE documents
  every tile, screenshot rendered) wired into CI. Headless suite now **249 checks**, all green.

  localStorage) and the Endings page now picks it up on arrival вҖ” so a real run drives the real
  endings. `tools/make-save-inspector.py` + `play/sample-save.json`.
- рҹ—әпёҸ **Saga Map** (`play/saga_map.html`) вҖ” the whole campaign on one page: the act spine across the
  eras, the conversations in each act, the flags each sets and gates on, the personal-quest lane,
  and the Court of the Dead fanning out to the six endings. **Every link deep-jumps into the
  matching explorer** вҖ” conversations into the Dialogue Viewer (`#id`), flags into the Flag Graph

  combat encounter with the full HUD (party roster, iso battlefield with move/threat tiles, attack

  (11, every deep-link resolves to a real conversation/flag). Headless suite now **238 checks**, all green.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.78.0 вҖ” *"The Wiring"* вҖ” the whole saga's flag graph, browsable

> The narrative engine runs on one `GameFlags` brain. This release renders that brain: a
> dependency graph of every story flag вҖ” what sets it, what gates on it вҖ” harvested from
> three independent sources and merged.

- рҹ•ёпёҸ **Flag Dependency Graph** (`play/flags_explorer.html`) вҖ” pick any of the **167 story flags**
  to see a bipartite map of what **writes** it (dialogue choices, quest resolutions, deeds, era
  content) and what **reads** it (ending gates, codex unlocks, dialogue conditions), each edge
  colour-coded by source. An **overview** panel surfaces the 27 domains, the most-connected *hub
  flags*, and the orphans вҖ” **write-only** (set but ungated: future headroom) and **read-only**
  (gated on but set by runtime systems like combat/losses/rests).
- рҹ§° `tools/extract-flags.py` merges three harvests: **C# `GameFlags` calls** (GetBool/GetInt = read,
  Set/AddInt = write) across `Assets/Scripts`, the **dialogue clause data** (`FlagClause`
  conditions/effects), and the **codex unlock flags** вҖ” into `play/flags-data.json`
  (**515 read/write edges**). `tools/make-flags-explorer.py` renders the page.
- рҹ§Ә `flags_explorer.test.js` (19 checks, incl. a parse-only JS compile and the marquee
  ending-gate вҶ’ Endings+codex dependency). Headless suite now **210 checks**, all green.

  & History) with category filters, each carrying the **GameFlags key** that unlocks it in-game and a

- рҹ’¬ **Dialogue Tree Viewer** (`play/dialogue_viewer.html`) вҖ” every conversation in the game as an

  (nodes / choices / `FlagClause` conditions+effects / `checkAbility`+`checkDC`+`failNodeId`) into
  `play/dialogue-data.json`. Reactive witness lines whose text is computed from flags are *marked*,
  not invented. `tools/make-dialogue-viewer.py` renders the page.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.70.0 вҖ” *"Sound and Fury"* вҖ” the game finds its voice (placeholder A/V)

> The longest-standing gap finally closed: audio and combat VFX were at 0%, so swings landed in silence
> over static cubes. Now every hit cracks, every heal chimes, every spell flashes, and each mode has an
> ambient bed вҖ” all fully synthesized in pure Python, no samples, no licenses. Honest placeholders: drop
> a real clip or frame with the same name to replace any of them.

- рҹ”Ҡ **14 SFX** (`hit`, `hit_<type>`, `crit`, `miss`, `heal`, `deed`, `levelup`) вҖ” stdlib `wave` synthesis.
- рҹ’Ҙ **9 VFX bursts** (`impact`, `impact_<type>`, `heal`, 6 frames each) вҖ” PIL, Sprite-imported, auto-played
  by `FxSystem` per damage type.
- рҹҺө **7 seamless ambient loops** (`Hub`, `Combat`, `Camp`, `Explore`, `Court`, `Vault`, `Fugue`) вҖ” sustained
  pads, click-free (whole-cycle partials), no melody to grate.
- Generators live in `tools/gen-placeholder-{sfx,vfx,music}.py`; committed raw (not LFS) with Unity `.meta`.
  **`tools/asset-check.sh`: 28% вҶ’ 89%.**

## рҹ‘‘ v3.69.0 вҖ” *"Every Step Optimal"* вҖ” A* pathfinding, proven least-cost

> The grid A* that moves every unit вҖ” hub click-to-move and tactical combat alike вҖ” is now proven not
> just *correct* but *optimal*: cross-checked against a brute-force Dijkstra oracle over 3,000 random
> weighted maps, so it can never quietly return a longer-than-necessary route.

- рҹ§ӯ **A* optimality pinned** вҖ” `play/pathfind.js` ports `Pathfinding.cs` 1:1 (4-connected, `moveCost`-
  weighted, Manhattan heuristic, step-onto-occupied-goal-but-never-through-bodies) and ships a Dijkstra
  oracle. `pathfind.test.js` (8 checks): straight line, wall detour, unreachable, unwalkable/occupied
  goal, difficult-terrain preference, `start==goal`, **plus a 3,000-map fuzz asserting A* cost == the
  Dijkstra optimum** (and agreement on unreachability). The fuzz caught an edge case on its first run.
- рҹ§Ә Headless verification suite now **139 checks** + the 400-game smoke, all green.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.68.0 вҖ” *"Quests Kept"* вҖ” the campaign spine, pinned headless

> Quest progression is the spine of the campaign, and its trickiest behaviour вҖ” objectives that complete
> the instant a flag flips, completion vs. *failure* precedence when both land at once вҖ” lived only in
> PlayMode, where this repo's CI can't reach. That reactive brain is now pinned in fast headless CI.

- рҹ§ӯ **Quest state machine pinned** вҖ” `play/quests.js` + `quests.test.js` (15 checks, CI-gated) model
  `QuestManager`/`Quest`: explicit start (once), objectives that fire only when *their* flag flips true
  while Active, `completionFlag` вҶ’ Completed, `failureFlag` вҶ’ Failed, **failure beats completion when both
  are true** (the C# checks failure first and `continue`s), Active-only reactions, quest isolation, and
  export вҶ’ import across managers (the save path).
- рҹ§Ә Headless verification suite now **131 checks** + the 400-game smoke, all green.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.67.0 вҖ” *"The Save Holds"* вҖ” pinning the serialization contract

> The least glamorous, most important kind of test: proof that your 20-hour run survives a save/load.
> `SaveSystem` flattens the story brain (GameFlags) into the parallel key/value lists JsonUtility needs;
> a one-element desync there would silently corrupt every save. That contract is now nailed down.

- рҹ’ҫ **Save round-trip pinned** вҖ” `play/save.js` + `save.test.js` (CI-gated): `GameFlags вҶ’ flattened
  DTO вҶ’ JSON вҶ’ back` is lossless across empty state, both bool values, int edges (`0`, `Вұ2ВіВ№`), 250
  keys with **key/value-list lockstep assertions**, dotted/spaced/unicode keys, re-save freshness, and
  double-round-trip stability. Plus 3 on-disk `SaveSystemTests` (re-save overwrites not stacks, a
  200-flag round-trip, int edge values).
- рҹ§Ә Headless verification suite now **116 checks** + the 400-game smoke, all green.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.66.0 вҖ” *"The Odds Against"* вҖ” threat forecasts, asset tooling, and the state of the game

> The forecast learns to look both ways: alongside "what are my odds of killing it," the HUD can now
> answer **"what are the odds it kills *me*?"** вҖ” exact incoming damage and down-chance from every foe
> in reach, computed by convolving real damage distributions, not guessed. Plus the operational answer
> to "what do I need to ship this?": an asset-completeness checker and an evidence-based report.

- рҹӣЎпёҸ **Threat forecasts** (`ThreatForecast`): mean incoming damage and the true probability the target
  drops this round (miss/crit/save-for-half all modeled). Pinned by `ThreatForecastTests` with a
  40k-seed Monte-Carlo cross-check against the real resolver, mirrored in `play/threat.js` (CI-gated),
  and live in the playable demo ("вҡ  incoming ~14 В· 38% down").
- рҹ§° **`tools/asset-check.sh`**: scans `Resources/` against the exact names the engine loads and reports
  what's present vs missing per category вҖ” run it after dropping in any pack.
- рҹ—әпёҸ **`docs/STATE_OF_THE_GAME.md`**: a full flow audit found the game **complete in code** (23/23
  systems wired, zero stubs, boot вҶ’ creation вҶ’ hub вҶ’ quests вҶ’ combat вҶ’ 5 eras вҶ’ 6 endings); the real
  remaining gaps are a human Unity run, audio+VFX (0%), and a distributable build.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.65.0 вҖ” *"The Odds Made Plain"* вҖ” Unity 6.4, the verified slice, and combat forecasts

> The engine moves to **Unity 6000.4.9f1**, the codebase gets its first full audit, and the game
> learns to tell you the truth before you swing: an **XCOM-style forecast** вҖ” hit %, crit %, expected
> damage, kill % вҖ” on every target, computed from the same math the dice roll. Alongside it, the
> combat and narrative cores now run **outside Unity** in a browser-playable slice, pinned by 100+
> ported tests so nothing can drift silently again.

- рҹҺҜ **Attack forecasts** (`AttackForecast`): analytic hit/crit/damage/lethal preview mirroring
  `AttackResolver` exactly вҖ” proven by a Monte-Carlo cross-check (40k seeded rolls per matchup) in
  `AttackForecastTests`. Toggleable via the new `ShowHitChance` setting.
- рҹҺӣпёҸ **QoL settings**: `ShowHitChance`, `ConfirmEndTurn`, `AutoEndTurn`, `AutosaveEnabled` (the
  campaign autosave now respects it), and `ScreenShake` вҖ” PlayerPrefs-persisted like the rest.
- рҹ§ӯ **Unity 6.4 migration**: every deprecated lookup replaced (`FindAnyObjectByType`, no-arg
  `FindObjectsByType`, `GetInstanceID` dropped), both `CS0252` reference-comparison warnings fixed,
  `ProjectVersion.txt` вҶ’ 6000.4.9f1 so CI tests on the engine the project ships on.
- рҹ©ә **The audit**: `CampaignBootstrap` no longer leaks its `OnFlagChanged` handler across
  defeat-restarts (zombie handlers could recruit stale companions into a new run); one-shot
  handlers in `EncounterBuilder`/`PrologueBootstrap`; `BreachDemo` unsubscribes too.
- вҡ–пёҸ **Balance canary retuned**: the reference Brute (Str 16, HP 34) brings the oracle into its own
  design bands вҖ” **Hero 70% [OK] В· Duelist 53% [OK]** (was 95/89 HIGH/HIGH).
- рҹ•№пёҸ **`play/` вҖ” the verified slice**: a browser-playable skirmish (Garrow, Roen, Varra vs the
  Returned) on a seed-faithful port of the combat rules, plus ports of endings, epilogue,
  inventory, and progression. **104 ported checks**, a prose-parity gate, a 500-playthrough fuzz,
  and a 400-game DOM smoke вҖ” wired into a new `combat-slice` CI workflow that re-runs whenever
  `Assets/Scripts/**` changes.
- рҹ§Ә **Epilogue coverage**: `EpilogueTests` (17 tests) pins the BG2-style payoff вҖ” slide gating,
  quest-outcome priorities, loved-and-lost, the anchor rule, the Chronicle.

## рҹ‘‘ v3.64.2 вҖ” *"The Skull Still Choosing"* вҖ” Aldric's fate, named at the forge

> The third cross-era callback, and the tightest loop in the saga: the **Time of Troubles** is the year
> Myrkul dies and his skull is beaten into the **Crown of Horns** вҖ” the very relic the gentle heretic
> **Aldric Morn** carries on his shelf in Act I. A new echo at that forge names what *you* saw of Aldric
> over tea, and turns it into a warning about the thing inside the crown.

- вҡ’пёҸ **A Keeper of the Bone Crown** (second echo in the Time of Troubles) reads your Act-I read of Aldric
  back to you, most-specific-first:
  - **Sensed the Crown using him** (`aldric.crown_doubt_planted`): "you caught the leash for what it was вҖ”
    do not unsee it."
  - **Named him a monster** (`aldric.named_monster`): "hate the relic, not the hand it chose for being kind."
  - **Saw the grieving father** (`aldric.grief_seen`): "love the size of his is the *door* the Crown was built
    to walk through."
  - **Made him say the count** (`aldric.cost_revealed`): "the crown keeps a *different* ledgerвҖҰ the line where
    the price is *him.*"
  - **Merely met him** (`aldric.met`): "the hammer here and the whisper there are the same throat."
  - **Never met him**: pure foreshadow вҖ” "a gentle hand will be offered this very crown and told it is a *means.*"
- рҹ§ұ **Reusable plumbing:** `SimpleEra` now supports a **second independent echo slot** (`echoGraph2` /
  `echoLabel2`), so any era can name more than one upstream thread. The Spellplague can pick up a second echo
  later for free.
- рҹӣЎпёҸ **Validated + tested:** the new graph is registered in `ContentValidator` (`era.echo_toot_crown`) and
  `EraEchoesTests` grows to **16 tests** (every branch + priority ordering). **29 suites В· ~201 tests.**
  Structural check green (165 C# files).

## рҹ•ҜпёҸ v3.64.1 вҖ” *"The Pulled and the Paid"* вҖ” the Breach, named downstream

> A direct extension of v3.64.0's cross-era callbacks: the single heaviest choice in the game вҖ” the
> **Breach** at the Wall of the Faithless вҖ” now echoes in the late eras, the same way the Crown Wars
> Verdict does. Also closes a reactivity gap: *walking away* from the Wall was previously invisible.

- вҡ–пёҸ **The Breach echoes forward.** Both late-era figures (the Time of Troubles **gravedigger** and the
  Spellplague **half-unmade soul**) now layer a third conditional thread on top of the Verdict + Netheril
  ones, keyed to what you did at the Wall:
  - **Pulled Maerin free** (`fugue.pull_maerin`): named as a *trade-death* вҖ” "the Wall never gives without
    takingвҖҰ carry them both, the pulled and the paid."
  - **Walked away** (`fugue.left_maerin`): named as counted restraint вҖ” "you did the arithmetic out loudвҖҰ
    it deserves a marker," and the soul that *would have been the cost* thanks you for it.
- рҹ©№ **Closed a reactivity gap (ROADMAP Tier 3 "every major choice leaves a trace"):** declining to pull
  Maerin set **no flag** before вҖ” the restraint was unwitnessed. It now sets `fugue.left_maerin`, so the
  choice is reactable (and is, immediately, by both echoes).
- рҹӣЎпёҸ **Tests:** `EraEchoesTests` grows to **10 tests** (added pulled/left/neither coverage for both eras).
  **29 suites В· ~195 tests.** Structural check green (165 C# files).

## вҸі v3.64.0 вҖ” *"The Source Remembers"* вҖ” Cross-Era Callbacks (the time-travel earns its keep)

> *A choice in -10,000 DR, spoken aloud in 1385 DR.* The saga's whole conceit is that you walk the
> hinge-points of history вҖ” so a verdict at the source should be **named** downstream, with its cost
> made visible. ROADMAP Tier 3 ("no choice forgotten") / DESIGN pillar V. **The last open Tier-3
> reactivity item lands.**

- рҹӘҰ **New `EraEchoes` content** вҖ” the *world itself* (not a companion) reacting to an upstream choice:
  - **Time of Troubles (1358 DR):** a **grey gravedigger** working the godless dead while the gods bleed
    speaks the **Crown Wars Verdict** back to you. Argue the damnation *down* (`crownwars.verdict_spared`)
    and the unclaimed get a resting-place "because of that single afternoon вҖ” the Wall was only ever a
    wall, never a furnace." Let it *pass* (`crownwars.verdict_passed`) and "the source remembers, even
    when the river forgets."
  - **Spellplague (1385 DR):** a **half-unmade soul** in the blue fire вҖ” held together only by being
    *witnessed* вҖ” thanks you (spared) or forgives you (passed) for that same verdict, ten thousand years on.
  - Both echoes append a **second thread** if you witnessed **Netheril's fall** (`netheril.cleared/arrived`)
    вҖ” the soot of the first apocalypse, the returned shades who "fell once before."
- рҹ§© **Reusable wiring:** `SimpleEra.echoGraph` (+`echoLabel`) places the beat as a Talk marker, mirroring
  the existing `witnessGraph` pattern; `CampaignBootstrap` wires both late eras. Built **live from the
  flags**, with a graceful neutral fallback if you witnessed neither upstream era.
- рҹӣЎпёҸ **CI-guarded:** both echo graphs registered in `ContentValidator` (broken-reference gate) and a new
  **`EraEchoesTests`** EditMode suite (**8 tests**) locks each branch вҖ” spared / passed / default /
  Netheril-thread вҖ” so the no-compiler sandbox still guards the reactivity. **29 suites В· ~193 tests.**
- рҹҹў Structural check green (**165 C# files**). Roadmap Tier 3 reactivity is now complete.

## рҹӣЎ v2.51.0 вҖ” *"Take Cover"* вҖ” Half-Cover for Ranged Attacks (CODE)

- рҹӣЎ **Cover** вҖ” a ranged attack against a target with another creature directly between it and the shooter
  (along an orthogonal or perfectly diagonal line) is made against **+2 AC** (half cover), with a *"COVER"*
  pop on a resulting miss. Deterministic aligned-line check (`AbilityRunner.HasRangedCover`), folded into
  `AttackResolver` via a `targetAcBonus`. Positioning now matters for archers and casters too. Phase B cover вң….
- рҹҹў 134 scripts / ~19.2k LOC, all clean.

  `faction.*.reputation` flags), each with a descriptive tier (known вҶ’ trusted вҶ’ honored, or marked вҶ’
  distrusted вҶ’ reviled). Shown only for factions that have noticed you. Phase C groundwork.
- рҹҹў 131 scripts / ~17.5k LOC, all clean.

## рҹӘЁ v1.87.0 вҖ” *"Shove"* вҖ” The Shove Action (CODE)

- рҹӘЁ **Shove action** вҖ” spend your action (key **V**, or the new HUD *"рҹӘЁ Shove"* button), then click an
  adjacent enemy: a **contested Strength check** pushes them one tile directly back if the space behind them
  is open. `TurnManager.TryShove` (uses `GridUnit.PlaceAt`). Battlefield control вҖ” break a flank, open a
  lane, or shove a foe off a wounded ally. Pairs with opportunity attacks and flanking.
- рҹҹў 131 scripts / ~17.5k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: action variety вҖ” Shove)

- рҹҺҜ **Enemy casters now aim area attacks smartly** вҖ” when an enemy's chosen ability is an `AreaBurst`, it
  centers the blast on the reachable party member whose tile catches the **most** of your party (tiebreak
  by proximity), instead of just hitting the nearest/weakest single target. Clumping up against a Fireball-
  toting foe now actually punishes you. `EncounterController.ChooseTarget`.

## рҹҸ· v1.83.0 вҖ” *"Read Your Kit"* вҖ” Richer Ability-Bar Labels (CODE)

## рҹ©№ v1.80.0 вҖ” *"Clean Slate"* вҖ” Reset Combat-Transient State Each Encounter (FIX)

- рҹ©№ **Bugfix:** the new per-combat flags (Dodge / Disengage / Help-advantage / last-reaction-round) lived
  on the `CharacterSheet` and weren't cleared between fights, so e.g. a unit that used its reaction in round
  1 of one battle could be denied its round-1 opportunity attack in the *next* battle. `TurnManager.StartCombat`
  now resets all four for every participant. Each encounter starts genuinely clean.
- рҹҹў 130 scripts / ~17.3k LOC, all clean.

## вң… v1.79.0 вҖ” *"Trust, but Verify"* вҖ” Validator Covers Abilities/Classes/Camp Content (CODE)

- вң… **`ContentValidator` extended** to sanity-check more data-only content: every ability (AreaBurst has a
  radius, heals have heal dice, no negative slot/range), every class's per-level kit resolves with no null
  entries, and camp **banters** / **night-talks** have unique ids/keys, both speakers, and non-empty lines.
  Catches the bug class the sandbox can't (no Unity compiler) вҖ” `ValidationDemo` reports PASS/FAIL on Play.
- рҹҹў 130 scripts / ~17.3k LOC, all clean.

## рҹ“– v1.78.0 вҖ” *"A Growing Spellbook"* вҖ” Per-Level Class Kits (CONTENT + CODE)

- рҹ“– **Classes now grow as they level.** `startingAbilities` was already a per-level unlock list but each
  class had only one entry; now every class has a curated kit that unlocks with level:
  - **Fighter:** Longsword вҶ’ Second Wind (bonus-action self-heal) вҶ’ Javelin вҶ’ Greataxe
  - **Wizard:** Fire Bolt вҶ’ Ray of Frost (slows) вҶ’ Thunderwave (Con-save burst) вҶ’ Fireball
  - **Cleric:** Mace вҶ’ Cure Wounds вҶ’ Bless вҶ’ Guiding Bolt вҶ’ Sacred Flame
  - **Rogue:** Dagger вҶ’ Shortbow вҶ’ Shortsword В· **Ranger:** Shortbow вҶ’ Dagger вҶ’ Longsword В· **Barbarian:** Greataxe вҶ’ Javelin
- вһ• New abilities (Second Wind, Ray of Frost, Sacred Flame, Guiding Bolt, Healing Word, Thunderwave,
  Javelin, Shortsword) and a **Slowed** status. Leveling up now meaningfully changes your options.

## вҶ” v1.76.0 вҖ” *"Flanked"* вҖ” Flanking Advantage (CODE)

- вҶ” **Flanking** (optional 5e rule) вҖ” a melee attacker gets **advantage** when an ally stands on the tile
  directly opposite them across the target. Pure positional check (`AbilityRunner.IsFlankingMelee`), folded
  into `AttackResolver` via an `extraAdvantage` input and logged with a *"is flanked!"* note. Rewards
  pincering a foe вҖ” and pairs with the new opportunity-attack / positioning layer.
- рҹҹў 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: cover & flanking)

---

## рҹҘҫ v1.75.0 вҖ” *"Disengage"* вҖ” The Disengage Action (CODE)

- рҹҘҫ **Disengage action** вҖ” spend your action (key **X**, or the new HUD *"рҹҘҫ Disengage"* button) so your
  movement this turn provokes **no opportunity attacks**. `TurnManager.TryDisengage()` вҶ’
  `CharacterSheet.IsDisengaging` (cleared at your next turn start, honoured by `Reactions`). Makes the new
  opportunity-attack layer something you can play around вҖ” the action economy now has a real retreat option.
- рҹҹў 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: action variety вҖ” Dodge/Dash/Help/Disengage complete)

---

## вҡЎ v1.74.0 вҖ” *"Don't Turn Your Back"* вҖ” Opportunity Attacks (CODE)

- вҡЎ **Opportunity attacks** вҖ” leave an adversary's melee reach (move from an adjacent tile to a non-adjacent
  one) without Disengaging, and that adversary spends its **reaction** (one per round) to make a free melee
  strike. New `Reactions.OnMoveCompleted`, hooked into both player and enemy movement; resolved via the new
  `AbilityRunner.ApplyOne` (which bypasses the action economy). `CharacterSheet.lastReactionRound` /
  `IsDisengaging` track the rules. Positioning suddenly matters.
- рҹҹў 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: reactions)

---

## рҹҢҖ v1.73.0 вҖ” *"DГ©jГ  Vu"* вҖ” A New-Game+ Camp Moment (CONTENT)

  will one day become the Lady in the Margins вҖ” gets an uncanny fireside moment: she feels the loop turn
  under her, *"I have run this proof before."* Ties the New-Game+ system to the story's deepest twist.
- рҹҹў 129 scripts / ~17.1k LOC, all clean.

- рҹ”ў **Round counter** вҖ” `TurnManager.RoundNumber` increments each time the initiative order wraps; logged
  at each round boundary and shown in the combat HUD's initiative header. Readability groundwork for
  duration/reaction features (status durations are already round-based).
- рҹҹў 129 scripts / ~17.1k LOC, all clean.

## рҹӨқ v1.71.0 вҖ” *"Help"* вҖ” The Help Action (CODE)

- рҹӨқ **Help action** вҖ” spend your action (key **T**, or the new HUD *"рҹӨқ Help"* button), then click an
  adjacent ally: their **next attack roll is made with advantage**. `CharacterSheet.HasHelpAdvantage`
  (consumed on the recipient's next attack-roll ability), `TurnManager.TryHelp()`, help-targeting mode in
  `PlayerCombatInput` (Esc cancels). Completes the Dodge/Dash/Help action trio.
- рҹҹў 129 scripts / ~17.1k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: action variety)

## рҹ§  v1.68.0 вҖ” *"Focus Fire"* вҖ” Smarter Enemy Targeting (CODE)

- рҹ§  **Enemy AI target selection** вҖ” instead of always charging the *nearest* hero, enemies now focus-fire
  the **lowest-HP foe they can actually reach and strike this turn** (finishing kills, concentrating
  damage), breaking ties by proximity; they fall back to closing on the nearest only when nothing is in
  reach. `EncounterController.ChooseTarget`. Combat reads sharper and punishes leaving a wounded unit exposed.
- рҹҹў 129 scripts / ~17.0k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: smarter enemy AI)

## рҹ’Ё v1.67.0 вҖ” *"Dash"* вҖ” The Dash Action (CODE)

- рҹ’Ё **Dash action** вҖ” spend your action (key **F**, or the new HUD *"рҹ’Ё Dash"* button) for extra movement
  equal to your speed this turn. `TurnManager.TryDash()`, surfaced in the combat HUD + Help (H) overlay.
  Builds on the Dodge action's economy pattern (Phase B: action variety).

## рҹӣЎ v1.65.0 вҖ” *"Defend"* вҖ” The Dodge Action (CODE)

- рҹӣЎ **Dodge / Defend action** вҖ” spend your action (key **G**, or the new HUD *"рҹӣЎ Defend"* button) and
  attack rolls against you are made at **disadvantage** until your next turn. Implemented as
  `CharacterSheet.IsDodging` (cleared at the dodger's next turn start), `TurnManager.TryDodge()`, factored
  into `AttackResolver`'s advantage math, and surfaced in the combat HUD + Help (H) overlay.
- рҹҹў 128 scripts / ~16.9k LOC, all clean. (ROADMAP near-term item #2 вң…)

## рҹҺҡпёҸ v1.48.0 вҖ” *"Sponge or Glass"* вҖ” Difficulty Now Scales Enemy HP (CODE)

> Difficulty scaled *damage* (v1.14); now it scales *durability* too, so Story/Hard feel distinct in
> length as well as lethality.

- рҹҺҡпёҸ **`GameSettings.EnemyHpMult`** (Story Г—0.8 В· Normal Г—1.0 В· Hard Г—1.3) applied at the campaign
  `Enemy()` builder, after HP is rolled вҖ” so every campaign foe and miniboss gets frailer or spongier to
  match the chosen mode. Pairs with the existing damage scaling for a real three-tier feel.
- рҹҹў 122 scripts / ~18.0k LOC, all clean.

## рҹ’ҫ v1.37.0 вҖ” *"Many Roads"* вҖ” A Save-Slot Manager (CODE)

> One autosave was fine for a prototype; a real CRPG wants parallel playthroughs. Now you can keep
> several, see what's in each at a glance, and pick which one the campaign writes to.

- рҹ’ҫ **`SaveSlotScreen` + `SaveSlots`** вҖ” **Load Game / Saves** off the main menu lists four slots
  (Autosave + Slot 1вҖ“3), each previewing **hero В· level В· current scene В· timestamp** via the new
  lightweight `SaveSystem.Peek` (no global state touched). Per slot: **Load**, **New Game** (overwrite,
  labeled), and a **confirm-guarded Delete** (`SaveSystem.Delete`).
- рҹҺҡпёҸ **Active-slot routing** вҖ” `SaveSlots.Active` (default `"save"`) now drives the campaign director's
  autosave and Continue, set when you pick a slot; `CampaignBootstrap.SaveSlot` reads it, so everything
  back-compat'd without touching the autosave path.

## рҹ•ҜпёҸ v1.30.0 вҖ” *"The Almshouse of the Unclaimed"* вҖ” A Second Explorable Lower City Room (CODE)

  builders), reached by a hub door once the prologue's cleared. Three reactive beats, all read live from

    child pulled behind a skirt, or a fevered hope you caused by speaking for the Unmade).

    heard your name.

  (`almshouse.token`); it earns a dedicated **`EndingResolver`** slide and a Chronicle line вҖ” the poor get
  someone *in the room* at the finale who promised they were real.

- рҹҹў 115 scripts / ~15.6k LOC, all clean. Act II is now somewhere you can *stand*, not just pass through.

> Act II's side content has been all moral conversation so far. This gives it *teeth*: the Faithless
> Choir thread escalates into an optional fight against a named leader, routed through the actual engine.

- вҡ”пёҸ **The Hollow Cantor** вҖ” once the street preaching is resolved (any way), a militant Choir cell

  `BuildChoirCellEncounter`): a tanky named leader, two Unmaking Zealots, two Sorrow-wraiths вҖ” built with
  the same `EncounterBuilder` flow the personal quests use, with full nameplates/floating-text/SFX.

  **+4 approval** with Garrow and Ilfaeril (you stopped a martyrdom before it started).

  slide ("you went down into the dark and broke it before it could make a martyr of anyone").

## рҹ§® v1.28.0 вҖ” *"Front to Back"* вҖ” Isometric Depth Sorting for Sprites (CODE)

> A small correctness fix that makes the v1.22 sprite seam actually *look* right: when art is present,
> units now layer by depth instead of fighting over who's drawn on top.

- рҹ§® **`IsoDepthSorter`** вҖ” added to each skinned unit's sprite; sets `SpriteRenderer.sortingOrder =
  -(x+y)*100` from world position every `LateUpdate`, so a unit lower/nearer on the iso diamond draws in
  front, and the order updates correctly as units move.
- рҹ”Ң Wired automatically by `UnitSpriteSkinner` (no extra setup); pure no-op until art exists.
- рҹ“„ `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`: unit-sprite row + checklist now note the live skinner + depth sort.
- рҹҹў 114 scripts / ~15.2k LOC, all clean. Drop in sprites and the battlefield reads with real depth.

## рҹ”Ҡ v1.27.0 вҖ” *"Give It a Sound"* вҖ” The Audio Seam (SFX + Music) (CODE)

> The last sense the game was missing. Same philosophy as the sprite, portrait, and VFX seams: silent
> until you drop a clip in a folder, then it *just plays.*

- рҹ”Ҡ **`AudioSystem`** вҖ” one-shot **SFX** from `Resources/SFX/` and looping **music** from
  `Resources/Music/`, self-bootstrapping a hidden persistent driver, no-op when a clip is missing. Master
  volume already rides `AudioListener.volume` (set from the Options slider), so it's governed for free.
- вҡ”пёҸ **Combat sound** вҖ” `AbilityRunner` plays **impact SFX by damage type** (`hit_fire`, `hit_ice`, вҖҰ,
  falling back to `hit`), plus `heal` and `miss` вҖ” right beside the floating numbers and hit VFX.
- рҹҺө **Music per mode** вҖ” the director's single `SwapMode` chokepoint swaps the loop by mode: **Hub,
  Combat, Camp, Fugue, Court, Vault, Explore**. A mode with no track keeps the current music rather than
  cutting to silence.
- рҹ“„ `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`: SFX & Music rows moved to **LIVE**, with the exact clip names.
- рҹҹў 114 scripts / ~15.1k LOC, all clean. Drop a folder of audio and the cube-game has a soundtrack.

## рҹ–јпёҸ v1.26.0 вҖ” *"A Face to the Voice"* вҖ” Dialogue Portraits (CODE)

> The art seam reaches conversations. Every line of the game already flows through one dialogue box вҖ”
> now that box can wear a face the instant you give it one.

- рҹ–јпёҸ **`WorldArt.Portrait`** вҖ” loads `Resources/Portraits/<speaker>` with a sensible fallback chain
  (full speaker name вҶ’ first word вҶ’ the unit's map sprite), cached, returning null when no art exists.
- рҹ—ЈпёҸ **`DialogueScreen`** draws a **portrait panel beside the conversation box**, captioned with the
  speaker, using `DrawTextureWithTexCoords` so both standalone and atlased sprites render correctly. No
  portrait present вҶ’ the box stands alone, exactly as before (fully graceful).
- рҹ§© **One face, many lines** вҖ” `Portraits/Doomguide.png` covers "Doomguide Knight", "Doomguide
  Enforcer", вҖҰ ; `Portraits/Tamsin.png` gives the crier a face; reuse a `Sprites/<name>.png` and it
  works for both the map unit and the dialogue.
- рҹ“„ `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`: portraits moved from "once a field is added" to **LIVE**.
- рҹҹў 113 scripts / ~15.0k LOC, all clean. Drop one PNG and a character looks you in the eye.

## рҹӘҰ v1.25.0 вҖ” *"The Wall Remembers"* вҖ” A Reactive Fugue Beat Before the Breach (CODE)

> Act II's mercy (or its absence) follows you past the world's edge. The grey waystation before the
> permanent loss now *answers* for how you treated the Gate's poor and dead вҖ” and warns, fairly, what
> the Breach will cost.

- рҹӘҰ **A Faithless soul in the Wall** (`FugueEra`) вҖ” a half-dissolved soul that greets you in one of three
  registers depending on your Lower City run: **grateful** (you freed the grave-tithe, paid the poor's
  debts, earned the quarter, gave the widow true comfort, or high standing), **bitter** (took a cut,
  silenced the Choir, or negative standing), or **wary-neutral**.
- вҡ–пёҸ **Fair foreshadowing of the Breach** вҖ” it spells out the Wall's arithmetic plainly ("the only way a
  soul comes *out* is if another goes *in* вҖҰ it takes the one nearest your heart"), seeding the romanceвҶ”
  Breach tithe before it lands вҖ” and even needles a corrupt player about haggling the toll down "to
  twenty percent."
- рҹ”§ Built **live from the flags each descent** (not at construction), so it always reflects the current
  playthrough; sets `fugue.soul.met`.
- рҹҹў 113 scripts / ~14.9k LOC, all clean. Act II's choices now reach all the way to the lip of the grave.

## вҡ°пёҸ v1.24.0 вҖ” *"The Tithe Collector"* вҖ” Who Pays for the Dead's Rest? (CODE)

> A fourth Act II side quest that points the game's central question вҖ” *what is a soul worth?* вҖ” straight
> at a marketplace: a man who sells the poor the right to a blessed grave.

- вҡ°пёҸ **New side quest вҖ” "The Tithe Collector"** (`ActTwoContent`) вҖ” Collector Vane charges the Gate's poor
  for consecrated rest; can't pay, and your dead wait Faithless in the pauper's pit. A **trilemma**:
  **[Persuasion DC 15] tear up the ledger** (Garrow вҶ‘вҶ‘, Lower City вҶ‘), **pay everyone's debts yourself**
  (generous; Garrow вҶ‘, Lower City вҶ‘), or **take a cut** (corrupt вҖ” Garrow вҶ“вҶ“, Ilfaeril вҶ“, Lower City вҶ“),
  with a graceful skill-fail branch and **two outcome-gated aftermath NPCs** (an empty table vs. a busy one).
- рҹ§ө **Reactive everywhere** вҖ” three new crier lines, a Journey/Lower City entry, a **Chronicle** line, and
  two **`EndingResolver`** epilogue slides (the pauper's pit blessed for free vs. piling up like Vane's
  ledger вҖ” "the Wall looked a little like his accounts").
- рҹҹў 113 scripts / ~14.8k LOC, all clean. Act II now carries **four** moral side quests, all braided into
  the crier, the journey, the chronicle, and the ending.

## рҹ§Ә v1.23.0 вҖ” *"Trust, but Verify"* вҖ” A Content-Integrity Validator (CODE)

> The sandbox has no Unity compiler, so the one bug class that can slip through is a mistyped node id in
> a conversation. This closes that gap: a smoke test that proves every dialogue link resolves.

- рҹ§Ә **`ContentValidator`** вҖ” walks every reachable authored `DialogueGraph` (all five personal quests via
  their `PersonalQuest` graphs, the three Act II side quests + crier + aftermaths, Aldric's tea, the
  Lady's two riddles) and reports **broken `nextNodeId`/`failNodeId`/`autoNextNodeId`/`startNodeId`,
  duplicate node ids, and empty/no-node graphs** вҖ” each with the exact graph + node.
- в–¶пёҸ **`ValidationDemo`** вҖ” one-click: runs it on Play and prints a **PASS/FAIL** report to the Console
  *and* on-screen (graph count, node count, every issue). Run it after editing dialogue.
- рҹҹў 113 scripts / ~14.6k LOC, all clean. The authored narrative now has a regression net.

---

## рҹҺЁ v1.22.0 вҖ” *"The Art Seam"* вҖ” Cubes Become Sprites the Moment Art Arrives (CODE)

> The cleanest possible on-ramp from "systems made visible" to "looks like a game": you don't touch a
> line of logic вҖ” you drop a PNG in a folder.

- рҹҺЁ **`UnitSpriteSkinner`** (on the campaign director) scans `GridUnit`s and, when `WorldArt` finds a
  matching sprite in `Resources/Sprites/`, **hides the placeholder cube and parents a camera-facing
  sprite billboard** (a new `CameraBillboard`) вҖ” keeping the collider so selection still works. No art
  present вҶ’ no change (graceful, exactly like the VFX system).
- рҹ—ӮпёҸ **Sensible lookup** вҖ” full display name вҶ’ first word вҶ’ faction, so **one `Sprites/Enemy.png`
  re-skins every foe at once**, while `Sprites/Garrow.png` upgrades her alone. No per-unit wiring.
- рҹ“„ Updated `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md` вҖ” В§2 goes from "PLANNED" to **"HOOK READY"** with the exact
  drop-in convention.
- рҹҹў 111 scripts / ~14.4k LOC, all clean. The seam between code and art is now a single folder.

## рҹ”ў v1.21.0 вҖ” *"Numbers That Fly"* вҖ” Floating Combat Text (CODE)

> The natural partner to the nameplates: now you don't just see *who's* hurt, you see the hit land.

- рҹ”ў **`FloatingCombatText`** вҖ” damage numbers, **+heals** (green), **MISS/RESIST** (grey), oversized
  golden **crits**, and condition names pop off the target, drift upward, and fade, with a cheap shadow
  for legibility. Self-bootstraps a hidden driver on first use; pure IMGUI, world-space, zero art.
- рҹҺҜ **Emitted at the source of truth** вҖ” `AbilityRunner` fires the right popup straight off the resolved
  `AttackResult` (after difficulty scaling), so it's correct everywhere combat happens: campaign, eras,
  demos. No per-encounter wiring.
- рҹҹў 110 scripts / ~14.3k LOC, all clean. With v1.20's nameplates, a cube-fight now reads at a glance.

## рҹӘ§ v1.20.0 вҖ” *"Faces in the Fray"* вҖ” World-Space Nameplates & HP Bars (CODE)

> The biggest *visible* upgrade yet, and a pure win for previewing in Unity: the colored cubes stop being
> anonymous. Now you can read a fight at a glance.

- рҹӘ§ **`UnitNameplates`** вҖ” a floating **name + faction-colored HP bar** over every `GridUnit`, projected
  to screen each frame, with the **active combatant highlighted** (gold в–¶ + outlined bar) and downed units
  greyed as "(down)". HP bar shades green вҶ’ amber вҶ’ red as it drops. Toggle with **N**.
- рҹ”Ң **Wired in where it matters** вҖ” added to the persistent campaign director (covers hub, combat, eras,
  every mode) and to `DemoBootstrap` (the flagship combat demo). Drop-in for any scene; it finds units itself.
- вқ” Added to the **Help** card and controls legend.
- рҹҹў 109 scripts / ~14.2k LOC, all clean. The systems-made-visible game just became *readable* at a glance.

## вҡ”пёҸ v1.19.0 вҖ” *"Knocked Out, Not Dead"* вҖ” Combat Consequences & a Breathing Bond (CODE)

> The last open roadmap item вҖ” approval that moves *in play* вҖ” plus a fix to an unintended cruelty: a
> companion downed in some random skirmish should not be gone forever. Only the Breach gets to do that.

- рҹ©№ **Stabilize-after-victory** вҖ” when the party wins, any **downed (0-HP) companion is pulled back from
  the brink** (revived to Вј HP), with a line in the log. Random battles no longer risk a permanent
  companion loss; **permanent death stays reserved for the Breach**, exactly as the story intends.
- вқӨпёҸ **Combat-time approval nudges** вҖ” surviving a fight together moves the meter: every fielded companion
  gains **+1 approval** on victory, and **+3** for anyone you had to pull back from the brink. Lives at the
  single combat-end chokepoint (`EncounterController.AwardExperience`), so it applies to **all** combat вҖ”
  campaign, eras, demos вҖ” keeping affinity breathing across the whole saga, not just in set-piece dialogue.
- рҹҹў 108 scripts / ~14.0k LOC, all clean. **The full companion roadmap is now complete.**

## рҹ•ҜпёҸ v1.18.0 вҖ” *"The Faithless Choir"* вҖ” The Unmade Comes to the Lower City (CODE)

> Act II stops being only personal errands and starts braiding into the *main* plot: the villain faction
> gets a face on a street corner, and your answer to it follows you to the Court.

- рҹ•ҜпёҸ **New side quest вҖ” "The Faithless Choir"** (`ActTwoContent`) вҖ” Brother Sere preaches the Unmade to
  the Gate's grieving poor, holding *you*, the Returned, up as proof the Wall can fall. A **trilemma**:
  **[Religion DC 15] give him doubt** (you've stood at the Wall; the cure is another atrocity вҖ” the
  nuanced best, +Ilfaeril/Garrow), **set the Fist on him** (suppress вҖ” Kelemvor вҶ‘, Lower City вҶ“, the
  grief just goes underground), or **speak for the Unmade** (`choir.sympathizer` вҖ” the Choir remembers
  who spoke for it; вҲ’Ilfaeril). With a graceful skill-fail branch.
- рҹ§ө **Reactive everywhere** вҖ” Tamsin the crier gains three new conditional lines for your Choir stance;
  the Journey screen's Lower City section and the Chronicle both track it; and `EndingResolver` adds a
  **Faithless-Choir epilogue slide** (doubt вҶ’ he sits with the dying; suppressed вҶ’ it surfaced harder;
  spoken-for вҶ’ they called you theirs).
- рҹҹў 108 scripts / ~13.9k LOC, all clean. The Lower City now reaches *up* into the central question, not
  just sideways into errands.

## рҹ“– v1.17.0 вҖ” *"The Chronicle of the Returned"* вҖ” A Run Summary, Any Time (CODE)

> A sprawling, reactive saga is hard to hold in your head. Now you never have to: one keystroke shows
> you the whole shape of your playthrough, and the ending recaps it as a capstone.

- рҹ“– **`ChronicleScreen` (press C)** вҖ” a persistent, press-anytime overlay (beside Options/Help) listing
  the run at a glance: **eras walked; who's still at your side, taken by the Wall, or walked away; quests
  resolved (N/5); hearts given; bonds broken; Lower City standing; the Lady's riddles; endings unlocked;
  difficulty.** Pure read of the flags via the new `EndingResolver.Chronicle()`.
- рҹҢ… **Recap at the close** вҖ” the **ending screen** now has a *"Read the Chronicle of the Returned"*
  expander, so the Court of the Dead leaves you with the whole journey, not just its last image.
- вқ” Added to the **Help** card (`H`) and the controls legend.
- рҹҹў 108 scripts / ~13.7k LOC, all clean. The saga is now legible in a single keystroke.

## рҹҸҷпёҸ v1.16.0 вҖ” *"The Quarter Pays Its Debts"* вҖ” Lower City Standing Reaches the Ending (CODE)

> The Act II reputation you build now follows you all the way to the Court of the Dead вҖ” the small good
> (or its absence) gets the last word it deserves.

- рҹӨқ **A reputation payoff** вҖ” once `reputation.lowcity` вүҘ 5, **Tamsin the crier** offers a one-time
  pledge (`lowcity.allies`): the Gate's poor, godless, and grieving will stand with you at the end. Gated
  via a `RequireIntAtLeast` conditional choice, so it only appears when earned and only once.
- рҹҢ… **It lands in the finale** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds a **Lower City epilogue slide**: a moving "they
  were there, with bread and lanterns and a hundred small refusals to look away" for high standing or the
  pledge вҖ” and a quiet, cutting "you spent them like coin" for negative standing.
- рҹ“ң **Legible** вҖ” the Journey screen's **Lower City** section now shows the pledge ("the quarter stands
  with you вҖ” they'll be there at the end").
- рҹҹў 107 scripts / ~13.5k LOC, all clean. Act II's small kindnesses now echo in the last accounting.

## рҹ§ӯ v1.15.0 вҖ” *"Never Lost, Never Stuck"* вҖ” Help Card & Autosave-on-Rest (CODE)

> Two small comforts that make a sprawling systems-game approachable: you can always find out what a key
> does, and you never lose much progress.

- вқ” **Help overlay** (`HelpOverlay`) вҖ” press **H** anytime, in any mode, for a scrollable reference card:
  world controls, battle controls, every hotkey screen (J/P/K/I/O/B), and saving. Lives on the persistent
  director object, so it's always one key away.
- рҹ’ҫ **Autosave on long rest** вҖ” resting at camp now autosaves (`CampScene.onRested` вҶ’ the director's
  `Autosave`), the natural CRPG checkpoint, with a "progress saved" note at the fire. Decoupled via a
  callback, so demos that use the camp don't touch the save file.
- рҹҹў 107 scripts / ~13.4k LOC, all clean.

## рҹҺҡпёҸ v1.14.0 вҖ” *"Your Table, Your Rules"* вҖ” Difficulty Modes (CODE)

> Some players are here for the tactics; some are here for the story and want the dice to get out of the
> way. Now both are first-class.

- рҹҺҡпёҸ **Story / Normal / Hard** (`GameSettings.Mode`) вҖ” chosen in the Options screen (off the menu or
  in-game with **O**), persisted via `PlayerPrefs`. **Story** softens enemy damage (Г—0.6) and buffs the
  party (Г—1.35); **Hard** sharpens enemy damage (Г—1.4) and nerfs the party a touch (Г—0.9); **Normal** is
  the intended 5e balance.
- рҹҺҜ **One chokepoint, applies everywhere** вҖ” scaling lives in `AbilityRunner` between resolve and apply,
  keyed off the target's faction, so it covers **all** combat: the campaign, every era, and every demo вҖ”
  no per-encounter wiring.
- рҹҹў 106 scripts / ~13.2k LOC, all clean. The table now flexes to the player at it.

---

## вҡ“ v1.13.0 вҖ” *"What You Stand To Lose"* вҖ” Romance вҶ” the Breach & the Finale Anchor (CODE)

> Love stops being a side-quest with a happy slide and becomes the highest-stakes choice in the game.
> Whoever you let yourself love is now who the Wall reaches for вҖ” and who the whole ending is *about.*

- вҡ°пёҸрҹ’” **The Wall takes what you love** вҖ” `ChooseBreachVictim` now, once Varra is safe (pact broken),
  is drawn to a **committed romance** (`romance.<id>.turn`) among the Breach candidates before falling
  back to a volunteer or the least-loved. Romancing someone makes the Breach a genuine stake for *them.*
- вҡ“ **The finale anchor** вҖ” `EndingResolver.AnchorId()` picks the face the cosmos rests on: the deepest
  romance (consummated вҶ’ committed вҶ’ the turn), or, lacking one, the companion you let in closest by
  approval. Every ending now closes on an **anchor beat** keyed to whether they're beside you, **lost to
  the Breach**, or **driven away** вҖ” three very different last words.
- рҹ’” **The cruelest epilogue** вҖ” a dedicated *"the one you loved, taken by the Wall"* slide (a bespoke
  Varra variant: "the receipt collected before you ever got to burn it"), separate from the generic loss
  slide, so a romanced Breach death lands with its full intended weight.
- рҹҹў 106 scripts / ~13.1k LOC, all clean. The game's tenderness and its cruelty now share one mechanism.

## рҹҸҷпёҸ v1.12.0 вҖ” *"The City Watches Back"* вҖ” Act II Side Content & a Reactive Lower City (CODE)

> Act II stops being a corridor between eras and starts being a *place.* The first pass at the hub's
> connective tissue: a world that reads your choices back to you, and small moral side quests whose
> stakes are reputation and conscience rather than loot.

- рҹҸҷпёҸ **`ActTwoContent`** вҖ” a Lower City content layer the hub places by flag-gate (active quest vs.
  resolved aftermath), the same way it gates Roen/Varra recruitment.
- рҹ“° **Tamsin, the street crier** вҖ” a living "news of you" board: her lines appear only as you *earn*
  them, via **conditional dialogue choices** (`DialogueChoice.conditions`) read live off `GameFlags` вҖ”
  the widow you helped, the Faithless man you freed (or didn't), the falling city you walked, the verdict
  you argued down, a romance the quarter is scandalised by, a companion who walked out.
- вҡ–пёҸ **Two thematic side quests**, dialogue-resolved (no grind):
  - **"The Widow's Coin"** вҖ” Mhaere's son was taken in the harvest, denied rest. A **kind lie**, the
    **hard truth** (Garrow approves), or an **[Insight DC 14]** *true* comfort that reframes remembrance
    as resistance to unmaking (the best вҖ” ties straight to the game's central question).
  - **"The Fist and the Faithless"** вҖ” a sergeant ordered to hand a godless beggar to the Doomguides.
    **[Persuasion DC 14]** free him (Garrow вҶ‘, Kelemvor вҶ“), **bribe** the paperwork away, or **uphold the
    law** (Kelemvor вҶ‘, Garrow & Ilfaeril вҶ“). Each moves `reputation.lowcity`.
- рҹ“ң **Journey legibility** вҖ” the **J** screen gains a **Lower City** section (standing + each side
  quest's outcome), so the new content reads as clearly as it plays.
- рҹҺ¬ **`ActTwoDemo`** вҖ” one-click: walk the hub, resolve a side quest, then re-ask the crier and watch the
  city's tale of you change.
- рҹҹў 106 scripts / ~13.0k LOC, all clean. The hub now *reacts.* (Next: deeper Act II вҖ” multi-room areas,
  Fugue-side beats, and tying side reputation into the finale.)

## рҹ’” v1.11.0 вҖ” *"The Bonds That Break"* вҖ” Rupture / Betrayal Arcs (CODE)

> The dark mirror of the romances. If love is a stake, this is the bill: drive a companion's approval into
> the ground вҖ” keep crossing the one line their whole self is built on вҖ” and the bond *frays.* The same
> data-first shape as the romances, pointed the other way.

- рҹ’” **Rupture engine** (`RuptureContent`) вҖ” five companions (Garrow, Roen, Varra, Naeve, Ilfaeril), each
  with a value-line that, crossed too often (approval вүӨ вҲ’25), triggers a **camp confrontation** in their
  own voice вҖ” desecration for Garrow, betrayed trust for Roen, the receipt for Varra, reckless reaching
  for Naeve, vengeance-wearing-mercy for Ilfaeril.
- рҹңҚ **Three outcomes, and amends has teeth** вҖ” **make amends** (only lands if you've earned *standing* вҖ”
  `HasStanding`: a night-talk shared or a romance spark; you can't talk back someone you never bothered
  to know вҶ’ `rupture.<id>.mended`, approval floored back up), **patch it over** (they stay, guarded вҶ’
  `rupture.<id>.uneasy`), or **let them walk** (`rupture.<id>.broken` + `companion.<id>.left`, removed
  from the party via `Party.Remove`). A thin amends that lacks standing collapses to patch-or-part.
- рҹ”Ҙ **Surfaced at the fire** вҖ” `CampScene` shows an urgent **"A Bond Frays"** section above everything
  else when `RuptureContent.Pending()` finds a cratered, present, unresolved companion.
- рҹҢ… **The Court remembers** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds a **walked-away epilogue slide** for any
  `companion.<id>.left` ("you'll never know how it ended for them вҖ” that is its own kind of loss").
- рҹҺ¬ **`RuptureDemo`** вҖ” one-click: a party with every bond cratered; two seeded with standing (amends can
  land), two without (words alone won't do it).
- рҹҹў 104 scripts / ~12.5k LOC, all clean. Love and its opposite now both have mechanical weight.

---

## вҡҷпёҸ v1.10.0 вҖ” *"Quality of Life"* вҖ” Options & a Legible Quest Log (CODE)

> A polish pass that makes the game *yours* to tune and the saga *legible* at a glance вҖ” the connective
> tissue a real player feels even when they never think about it.

- вҡҷпёҸ **Options screen** (`GameSettings` + `SettingsScreen`) вҖ” three knobs, persisted via `PlayerPrefs`
  and applied live: **ambient-banter toggle, master volume, dialogue text-speed** (or instant). Reachable
  off the main menu **and** in-game at any time with **O** (a persistent overlay above the mode root).
- вҢЁпёҸ **Typewriter dialogue** вҖ” `DialogueScreen` now reveals lines at the chosen chars/second, with a
  one-click "show the rest" to skip the reveal; honors the Instant-text setting. Wired to the live setting,
  so dragging the slider in Options changes the feel immediately.
- рҹ”Ү **Banter respects the setting** вҖ” `AmbientBanter` now checks `GameSettings.BanterEnabled` (the **B**
  quick-mute still works too).
- рҹ“ң **Quest-log beat tracking** вҖ” the Journey screen (**J**) now shows each companion quest's **current
  beat** (thread opened вҶ’ at the scene вҶ’ fought вҶ’ *resolved-how*, e.g. "doctrine on trial", "contract
  burned") and a new **Bonds** section tracking each romance's furthest stage (a spark вҶ’ trust вҶ’ the turn
  вҶ’ committed вҶ’ the last night).
- рҹҹў 102 scripts / ~12.1k LOC, all clean. The companion content now *reads* as clearly as it plays.
