## рҹ’һ v1.9.0 вҖ” *"The Slow Burns"* вҖ” All Four Romance Arcs (CODE)

> The companions stop being people you fight beside and become people you stand to *lose.* Four full
> romances, each an **argument about one of the game's themes** вҖ” so falling in love is also taking a
> position on what the game is about. Built data-first, the way the personal quests were.

- рҹ’һ **Romance engine** (`RomanceContent`) вҖ” a reusable, data-driven arc table on a shared six-stage
  spine: **Spark вҶ’ Trust вҶ’ Turn вҶ’ Crisis вҶ’ Choosing вҶ’ The Last Night.** Each beat is gated by **both** an
  approval threshold **and** progression вҖ” the previous stage, and for the **Crisis**, the companion's
  *resolved personal quest* (the romance literally runs through their quest). Mirrors `CampContent`: pure
  data, no scene boilerplate.
- рҹҺӯ **Four arcs, four themes** вҖ” **Garrow** (faith: something can be holy in a cruel cosmos), **Roen**
  (belonging: the bravest thing is to *stay*), **Naeve** (guilt: are you allowed to be loved after what
  you did), **Varra** (worth: you are more than your price). Key-beat dialogue drawn from
  `docs/story/16_ROMANCE_SCRIPTS.md`, each with a **deepen-or-stay-platonic** choice (holding is
  non-destructive вҖ” the beat waits for you).
- рҹ”Ҙ **Played at the fire** вҖ” `CampScene` gains a **"Grow Closer"** section beside the night-talks,
  surfacing the best-eligible beat (`RomanceContent.Best()`); choosing someone moves their approval.
- рҹңҚ **Love is a stake, not a collectible** вҖ” pursuing two romances past the **Turn** is gently
  disallowed (`CommittedElsewhere`); a single, in-character commitment.
- рҹҢ… **Epilogue payoffs** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds a bespoke slide per consummated romance, including the
  game's most devastating beats: **Garrow gives you your own last rite in Break the Loop**, **Naeve
  derives the rewritten Law beside you in Jergal's Keyhole**, **Roen at the niche with no joke left**,
  and **Varra burning the receipt** for her soul at last.
- рҹҺ¬ **`RomanceDemo`** вҖ” one-click tour: all four companions, gates pre-seeded, every arc open to walk.
- рҹҹў 100 scripts / ~11.8k LOC, all clean. **The companion pillar is whole: recruit вҶ’ banter вҶ’ approval вҶ’
  camp вҶ’ personal quest вҶ’ romance вҶ’ epilogue.**

---

## рҹ•ҠпёҸ v1.8.0 вҖ” *"The Vote"* вҖ” Ilfaeril's Personal Quest (& the Companion Pillar Complete) (CODE)

> The fifth and final companion arc on the v1.5.0 template вҖ” and with it, **all five companions now have
> a playable personal quest, end to end.** Ilfaeril faces the one soul he owes across ten thousand years,
> and the choice you help him make is the one his whole being turns on: *is atonement allowed to end?*

- рҹ•ҠпёҸ **Ilfaeril's quest вҖ” "The Vote"** (`IlfaerilQuestContent`) вҖ” an ancient elven reliquary, its lock
  keyed to **Maerith of the Singing Vale**, one of the souls his Crown-War council voted to *unmake* вҖ”
  the verdict that hardened into the **Law of the Faithless.** Its waking draws the **Choir of the
  Unmade**, who revere him as their first witness and offer to end his guilt by proving he never should
  have felt any. Three hand-written conversations (arrival / the Pale Cantor / the resolution).
- рҹңҚ **A moral trilemma** keyed to his wound (*atonement is not self-erasure; he is allowed to stop
  paying*): **refuse her forgiveness** and guide the lost forever (+10, devotion that is also a kind of
  hiding), **accept it** and let himself be more than his worst vote (+20, the Oath of Redemption
  fulfilled), or an **[Insight DC 16]** gambit that hears her forgiveness for what it is вҖ” *not a door,
  a sword held hilt-first* вҖ” and turns it into a **commission to tear the Wall open for the rest of her
  people** (+30, forgiveness that puts a man back to work) вҖ” with a graceful fail branch. *(First quest
  to gate on Wisdom/Insight rather than Cha/Int.)*
- вҡ”пёҸ **The Choir, come for the witness** вҖ” a five-enemy encounter (the Pale Cantor, two Choir Heralds,
  two Unmaking Acolytes) routed through the director, returning to the crypt for the resolution on victory.
- рҹҢ… **Epilogue payoff** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds an **Ilfaeril slide** keyed to his choice (commission /
  forgiven / penance), alongside the other four.
- рҹӘқ **Hub thread now playable** вҖ” Ilfaeril's reliquary hook (`CompanionQuests`) flips to `playable =
  true` with a `followLabel`; also fixed a pronoun slip in its tease (canon: *he* renounced his house).
- рҹҺ¬ **`IlfaerilQuestDemo`** вҖ” one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- рҹҹў 98 scripts / ~11.3k LOC, all clean. **The companion-quest pillar is complete: five for five.**

---

## вңЁ v1.7.0 вҖ” *"After the Sky Fell"* вҖ” Naeve's Personal Quest (CODE)

> The fourth companion arc, again almost pure content on the v1.5.0 template: Naeve goes home to a
> fragment of Netheril that never finished falling вҖ” and the choice you help her make is the one her
> whole wound turns on: *some mistakes can only be carried, not erased.*

- вңЁ **Naeve's quest вҖ” "After the Sky Fell"** (`NaeveQuestContent`) вҖ” a shard of dead Weave hums her
  home's exact note: a piece of the **Seventh Enclave**, held aloft a thousand years past its death by a
  failing **mythallar**. The echo of the **Steward Vaelin** tells her the truth вҖ” *her own* wardstone
  saved this fragment by sentencing it to fall slowly, and keeping it frozen has been draining the last
  live Weave in the world. Three hand-written conversations (arrival / Vaelin's echo / the resolution).
- рҹҢҢ **A moral trilemma** keyed to her wound (*her genius ended a world; she must learn to carry, not
  erase*): **freeze the shard in stasis** and keep the last of Netheril whole (+10, a tomb she calls a
  home), **let it finish falling** and carry the grief instead of the wreckage (+20, acceptance), or an
  **[Arcana DC 16] gambit** that opens the wardstone and gives its live Weave *back to the present* as a
  seed instead of a shroud (+30, "an arithmetic that builds") вҖ” with a graceful fail branch that
  collapses to the two plain choices. (A faint *you-are-a-loop* foreshadow hides in the margin note.)
- вҡ”пёҸ **The last protocol** вҖ” a five-enemy encounter (a Mythallar Ward, two Arcane Sentinels, two
  Weave-wraiths) routed through the director, returning to the core for the resolution on victory.
- рҹҢ… **Epilogue payoff** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds a **Naeve slide** keyed to her choice (rekindled /
  released / preserved), alongside Roen's, Varra's, and Garrow's.
- рҹӘқ **Hub thread now playable** вҖ” Naeve's shard hook (`CompanionQuests`) flips to `playable = true`
  with a `followLabel`, opening the quest through the existing generic hub wiring.
- рҹҺ¬ **`NaeveQuestDemo`** вҖ” one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- рҹҹў 96 scripts / ~11.0k LOC, all clean. **Four playable companion quests; one to go.**

---

## вҡ–пёҸ v1.6.0 вҖ” *"A God-Shaped Hole"* вҖ” Garrow's Personal Quest (CODE)

> The third companion arc, built almost entirely from content on the v1.5.0 template: Sister Garrow is
> summoned to a Kelemvorite tribunal for heresy, and the choice you help her make is the one the whole
> saga is really about вҖ” *what is a soul worth that no god ever claimed?*

- вҡ–пёҸ **Garrow's quest вҖ” "A God-Shaped Hole"** (`GarrowQuestContent`) вҖ” a black-edged writ calls Sister
  Garrow to a Doomguide tribunal to answer for failing to lay her fallen mentor and for travelling with
  **the Returned** вҖ” a soul no god claimed. **Justiciar Veld**, who taught her catechism, means to make
  her recant or be cast out; the trial is rigged, the verdict pre-written, so it becomes a fight. Three
  hand-written conversations (arrival / the Justiciar's charge / the resolution).
- рҹңҚ **A moral trilemma** keyed to her wound (*obedience that felt like betrayal*): **recant to keep the
  grey** and do the work from inside (+10, a brittle, sorrowful faith), **walk away from the faith
  entirely** and lay the dead under no one's law (+20, Faithless and unafraid), or a **[Religion DC 16]
  gambit** that puts Kelemvor's *own canon* on trial вҖ” proving the Faithless judgment is itself the
  heresy (+30, the seed of the rewritten Law) вҖ” with a graceful fail branch that collapses to the two
  plain choices.
- вҡ”пёҸ **The Justiciar's tribunal** вҖ” a five-enemy encounter (Veld, two templar inquisitors, two grey
  enforcers) routed through the director, returning to the temple for the resolution on victory.
- рҹҢ… **Epilogue payoff** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds a **Garrow slide** keyed to her answer (reformer /
  apostate / brittle keeper), alongside Roen's and Varra's.
- рҹӘқ **Hub thread now playable** вҖ” Garrow's summons hook (`CompanionQuests`) flips to `playable = true`
  with a `followLabel`, so the existing generic hub wiring opens the quest with no bespoke code.
- рҹҺ¬ **`GarrowQuestDemo`** вҖ” one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- рҹҹў 94 scripts / ~10.8k LOC, all clean. **Three playable companion quests; the template keeps delivering.**

---

## вҡ–пёҸ v1.5.0 вҖ” *"The Bill Comes Due"* вҖ” A Reusable Quest Engine & Varra's Arc (CODE)

> The personal-quest pattern becomes a *template*: one data-driven scene now runs every companion's
> arc, and Varra's is the first new quest built on it вҖ” an infernal contract, not a sibling rescue.

- рҹ§© **`PersonalQuestScene` + `PersonalQuest`** вҖ” Roen's bespoke scene is refactored into a **reusable,
  data-driven stage**. The arc shape (arrive вҶ’ examine вҶ’ confront вҶ’ fight вҶ’ moral call вҶ’ leave) is now
  code; *what* happens is config. Each remaining companion quest is mostly **content, not boilerplate.**
- вҡ–пёҸ **Varra's quest вҖ” "The Bill Comes Due"** (`VarraQuestContent`) вҖ” her patron calls the contract she
  signed at **six years old**, early. In a deconsecrated chapel, the cambion broker **Quill** who sold
  her waits to collect. A fight (Quill + contract-devils + imps of the fine print) and a **moral
  trilemma**: **carry her debt yourself** (+25, she sleeps for the first time in 20 years), **let her
  burn it freely** (+15, her choice, her clock), or an **[Arcana DC 16] loophole** that binds her
  *patron* instead (+30, the best outcome) вҖ” with a graceful fail branch.
- рҹҢ… **Epilogue payoff** вҖ” `EndingResolver` adds a **Varra slide** keyed to your call (patron-bound /
  debt-taken / freed), alongside Roen's Wrenna slide.
- рҹӘқ **Generic hub threads** вҖ” the hub now places a "follow the thread" marker for **any** playable,
  started-but-unresolved companion quest (`CompanionQuests.playable`), wired through a single
  `onEnterPersonalQuest(id)` callback. Roen's old bespoke wiring is gone.
- рҹҺ¬ **`VarraQuestDemo`** вҖ” one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- рҹ§№ Removed the now-redundant `RoenQuestScene` (folded into `PersonalQuestScene`).
- рҹҹў 92 scripts / ~10.6k LOC, all clean. **Two playable companion quests; a template for the rest.**

---

## рҹ—ЎпёҸ v1.4.0 вҖ” *"The Honest Lie"* вҖ” Roen's Personal Quest, End to End (CODE)

> The first companion thread becomes a *playable arc*: a silent Harper safehouse, a sister who lied
> for two years to keep her brother off the Wall, a Doomguide cell, and a moral call that follows you
> all the way to the epilogue. The hook from v1.3.0 now has a quest on the end of it.

- рҹ—әпёҸ **`RoenQuestScene`** вҖ” a bespoke arc on the SimpleEra pattern with its own beat order: **arrive** at
  the safehouse (auto-dialogue), examine the scene, **corner Wrenna** for the reveal, fight, then make
  the call. State-driven by `roen.quest.cleared` (the fight) and `quest.roen.resolved` (the choice).
- рҹ“ң **`RoenQuestContent`** вҖ” three hand-written conversations (Arrival, the Wrenna reveal, the
  Resolution) with a real **moral trilemma**: **forgive** her (Roen **+20** approval, Wrenna saved),
  **condemn** her by the rules (**вҲ’15**, a Harper intel boon), or a **[Persuasion DC 15] gambit** to
  turn her into a double agent (best outcome: **+25**, both boons) вҖ” with a graceful fail branch.
- вҡ”пёҸ **The Doomguide cell** вҖ” a six-enemy encounter (knights, enforcers, a zealot, an interrogator)
  routed through the director, returning you to the safehouse for the resolution on victory.
- рҹҢ… **Epilogue payoff** вҖ” `EndingResolver` now adds a **Wrenna slide** keyed to your call, so the
  safehouse choice echoes in the Court of the Dead (saved / double-agent / turned-in variants).
- рҹӘқ **Hub thread** вҖ” once you've examined the cipher hook, a *"Follow the cipher"* marker opens the
  quest; it closes once resolved. Wired into the director (`EnterRoenQuest` / `StartRoenFight`).
- рҹҺ¬ **`RoenQuestDemo`** вҖ” one-click preview (skips the battle) to tour all three resolutions.
- рҹҹў 89 scripts / ~10.0k LOC, all clean. **The first companion quest is fully playable.**

---

## рҹ§ө v1.3.0 вҖ” *"Threads to Pull"* вҖ” Approval in Play & Companion Personal-Quest Hooks (CODE)

> The affinity loop closes end-to-end: kindness now *moves the meter in normal play*, and opening
> someone up at the fire hangs a thread in the world вҖ” the start of their personal quest.

- вқӨпёҸ **Approval-shifting dialogue** вҖ” the Roen and Varra recruit conversations now **grant approval**
  through `companion.<id>.approval` (warmer choices give more), so the meter rises in ordinary play вҖ”
  not just demos. The kindness вҶ’ approval вҶ’ camp night-talk loop now runs **without scaffolding.**
- рҹ§ө **Companion personal-quest hooks** (`CompanionQuests`) вҖ” once a campfire **night-talk** opens a
  companion up, a pointer to their **Act II personal quest** appears in the hub (Roen's Harper cipher,
  Varra's matured invoice, Garrow's heresy summons, Naeve's shard of dead Weave, Ilfaeril's reliquary).
  Examining it **starts the quest** (`quest.<id>.started`) and reads its hand-written tease.
- рҹӘқ **`Interactable.onExamined`** вҖ” examine markers can now fire a code callback (used to flag quest
  starts); a small, reusable hook for any "inspecting this *does* something" beat.
- рҹ“ң **Journey tracker** now lists a **Companion Threads** section вҖ” which personal quests you've opened
  and started вҖ” so the new content is legible at a glance (press **J**).
- рҹҹў 86 scripts / ~9.5k LOC, all clean.

---

## рҹ”Ҙ v1.2.0 вҖ” *"The Fire's Low"* вҖ” Camp, Long Rest & Approval-Gated Night-Talks (CODE)

> The quiet half of a CRPG. A place to rest your wounds and refill your magic вҖ” and a campfire
> where the companion who trusts you most finally says what they've been carrying.

- рҹ”Ҙ **`CampScene`** вҖ” a campfire mode reached from a **new hub marker**: a **long rest** restores the
  fielded party to **full HP** and **refreshes all spell slots**, and a **"sit with someone"** beat
  offers a night-talk from whichever companion is closest to you.
- рҹ’¬ **Approval-gated night-talks** (`CampContent`) вҖ” five hand-written monologues (Roen, Varra, Garrow,
  Naeve, Ilfaeril), each unlocked only once that companion's **approval crosses a threshold** *and*
  they're **fielded**. One per companion; listening itself earns a little more approval. The new
  approval meter (v1.1.0) now *pays off.*
- рҹҺ¬ **`CampDemo`** вҖ” one-click: a battle-worn party at the fire with approval pre-seeded and a wounded
  companion, so you can watch the rest heal them and hear a night-talk immediately.
- рҹҹў 84 scripts / ~9.3k LOC, all clean.

---

## рҹ“– v1.1.0 вҖ” *"What You've Witnessed"* вҖ” The Codex, Companion Sheets & Ambient Banter (CODE)

> The world starts talking back. A compendium that fills in as you witness the saga, full stat
> blocks for your companions (with how much they *like* you), and idle chatter on the road.

- рҹ“– **`CodexScreen`** (press **`K`**) вҖ” a lore & bestiary compendium with a category rail (The Premise,
  The Four Masks, Bestiary, Lore & History) and a reading pane. Entries live in **`CodexContent`** and
  are **gated by `GameFlags`** вҖ” you only know what you've witnessed, so the Codex *grows as you play*
  (Aldric unlocks at tea, the Unmade at Netheril, the Last Returned at the Crown Wars, the Lady at the
  Reader's BoonвҖҰ). Shows **N/total discovered.**
- рҹӣЎпёҸ **Companion sheets** вҖ” the Party screen (**`P`**) now expands on click: full **ability block**
  (STRвҖ“CHA with modifiers), **AC / HP / initiative / proficiency**, and an **approval meter** showing
  how much each companion likes you (devoted вҶ’ hostile), read from `companion.<id>.approval`.
- рҹ’¬ **`AmbientBanter`** вҖ” idle party chatter while you wander, drawn from **`PartyBanter`** and filtered
  to **who's actually in the field** (Roen, Varra, Garrow, Naeve, Ilfaeril each have voice; plus eerie
  anyone-lines about the Wall). Fades in low in the frame; **mute with `B`.**
- рҹ”– **Codex hooks** вҖ” `EnterVault` now sets `riddle.entered` so the Vault of Tens self-documents.
- рҹҹў 82 scripts / ~9.1k LOC, all clean.

---

## рҹҸӣпёҸ v1.0.0 вҖ” *"The Saga, Made Legible"* вҖ” Journey Tracker, Roster Management & the Vertical-Slice Capstone (CODE)

> The slice now reads as a *game with a spine*: a quest log that tracks the whole arc, a party
> bench, a finale that's earned rather than handed to you, and a player-facing how-to-play guide.

- рҹ“ң **`JourneyScreen`** (press **`J`**) вҖ” a live **quest tracker** read straight out of `GameFlags`:
  the Cinderhaunt, tea with Aldric, the Breach, all **four eras**, the **Vault of Tens**, and the
  **Reader's Boon** вҖ” each вң”/в—Ӣ вҖ” plus **"Endings unlocked: N/6"** and a **вҳ… golden road** indicator
  when one of the two deepest endings is reachable. The saga finally reads as a checklist.
- рҹӣЎпёҸ **`RosterScreen`** (press **`P`**) вҖ” **bench/field** any recruited companion up to `maxActive`;
  the **protagonist is locked into the field.** Benched companions keep their levels and gear.
- рҹҸӣпёҸ **Finale gating tightened** вҖ” the **Court of the Dead** now opens only after you've **walked at
  least one era** (`netheril.cleared`), so the ending is a *culmination*, not a shortcut. The Journey
  screen tells you exactly why it isn't open yet.
- рҹ“ҳ **`docs/HOW_TO_PLAY_THE_SLICE.md`** вҖ” a 20-minute guided run from the title screen to the Court of
  the Dead: the loop step-by-step, the full control map, and how to read the Journey & Party screens.
- рҹҹў 78 scripts / ~8.8k LOC, all clean. **Boot вҶ’ New Game вҶ’ play the whole arc, now with a quest log.**

---

## рҹҺӣпёҸ v0.9.3 вҖ” *"A Front Door"* вҖ” Main Menu, Continue, Roaming Tally & Sprite-Ready Units (CODE)

> The wrapper that turns a pile of demos into a *game you boot up.*

- в–¶пёҸ **`MainMenu`** вҖ” a real front end: **New Game / Continue / Quit.** Drop it in the boot scene; it
  launches `CampaignBootstrap` fresh or resumes the save.
- рҹ’ҫ **Save & Continue, deepened** вҖ” the save now captures the **hero's build** (name, class, race,
  level, ability scores); the campaign **autosaves on every return to the hub**, and **Continue**
  reconstructs the hero *and* re-recruits your roster from the `companion.*.recruited` / `.lost` flags
  (permanent losses stay lost вҖ” the Wall keeps what it took, across sessions).
- рҹҺІ **Roaming Tally** вҖ” after you've walked an era, the Lady in the Margins **pops in at the hub**
  (G-Man style) with a one-off roaming riddle; answer it for her amusement. Appears once.
- рҹ–јпёҸ **Sprite-ready units** вҖ” `WorldArt` + a `GridUnit` hook: drop `Resources/Sprites/<Name>.png` and
  that character renders as a sprite billboard instead of a cube вҖ” *zero wiring.* No art? Cubes, as
  before. The bridge from prototype to a real CRPG look.
- рҹҹў 76 scripts / ~8.7k LOC, all clean. **Boot вҶ’ New Game вҶ’ play the whole arc вҶ’ Continue later.**

---

## рҹҢ«пёҸрҹҢҖ v0.9.2 вҖ” *"Where the Ink Runs"* вҖ” The Last Two Eras (CODE)

> All four time-travel eras are now playable вҖ” and the Spellplague makes *causality itself* a hazard.

- рҹ§© **`SimpleEra`** вҖ” a reusable, config-driven era scene (grid + floor + camera + exploration UI +
  leader + a point-of-interest + a battle trigger), so new eras are *config, not boilerplate.*
- рҹҢ«пёҸ **Time of Troubles** (era 3, 1358 DR) вҖ” witness the **Crown of Horns forged from Myrkul's skull**;
  the Crown-is-Myrkul reveal lands in-engine (sets `act4.crown_is_myrkul`). Fight the avatar-touched.
- рҹҢҖ **Spellplague** (era 4, 1385 DR) + **`SpellplagueHazard`** вҖ” a *causality-optional* battlefield:
  each turn after the second may **swap two combatants' positions** (a reality skip) and lash a random
  one with **blue fire** (Force). Your positioning is never quite safe. `EncounterBuilder` gains a
  `spellplagueHazard` toggle.
- рҹ”— Both wired as flag-gated hub rifts (ToT after the Crown Wars; Spellplague after ToT). The director
  is now a **10-mode** machine. Plus **`SpellplagueDemo`** for a one-click taste.
- рҹҹў 74 scripts / ~8.4k LOC, all clean. **All four eras of the saga are playable.**

---

## рҹҢ… v0.9.1 вҖ” *"The Court of the Dead"* вҖ” The Six Endings, In Code

> The capstone that makes every flag *mean* something: a finale that reads your whole playthrough.

- рҹ§  **`EndingResolver`** вҖ” pure logic that reads GameFlags to decide which endings you've **earned the
  right to choose** (deeper truths gate the golden roads: *Jergal's Keyhole* needs the Lady's riddle +
  a spared Verdict; *Break the Loop* needs you to have grasped the loop), supplies each ending's prose,
  and assembles **BG2-style epilogue slides** keyed to who lived, who the Wall took, the Verdict, the
  Lady's witness, and Aldric's fate.
- рҹҸӣпёҸ **`EndingScreen`** вҖ” the **Court of the Dead** finale: the convergence framing, the available
  endings as choices (golden ones starred), and on a pick the full prose + epilogue.
- рҹ”— Wired in: a **Court of the Dead** exit in the hub (now an **8-mode** director), plus **`EndingDemo`**
  вҖ” a one-click tour that unlocks all six to read prose + epilogues side by side.
- рҹҹў 70 scripts / ~8.0k LOC, all clean. The full arc вҖ” create вҶ’ play вҶ’ *end* вҖ” now exists in code.

## вҡ°пёҸ v0.9.0 вҖ” *"The Wall Keeps What It Takes"* вҖ” The Fugue, Maerin & the Breach (CODE)

> The game's first **permanent loss** вҖ” the beat that proves this story will take things and never
> give them back.

- рҹ©¶ **`FugueEra` + `FugueContent`** вҖ” descend (from the hub, after the Cinderhaunt) into the grey
  **Fugue Plane** and walk the **Wall of the Faithless**: the faces in the mortar, and the niche with
  **your own name**, a little more formed than last time.
- вҡ°пёҸ **The Breach** вҖ” pull **Maerin** free of the Wall, and the Wall takes its tithe: a companion is
  **removed from the party forever** (`Party.Remove`; no revival exists, by design). *Who* is decided
  by an **authored-fate** system (doc 15): **Varra** by default (her Act I 'leash' pays off), else a
  companion **volunteers** (Ilfaeril вҶ’ Garrow вҶ’ Naeve), else the **lowest-approval** member вҖ” so the
  grief is *authored by your earlier care*, not merely inflicted.
- рҹ§‘вҖҚрҹӨқвҖҚрҹ§‘ **Two more recruitable companions** вҖ” **Varra** (a tiefling warlock, in the hub) and **Maerin**
  (pulled from the Wall) вҖ” bringing the playable roster to six, all flag-driven.
- рҹҺ¬ **`BreachDemo`** вҖ” a one-click harness: walk the Fugue, pull Maerin, watch Varra be taken.
- рҹ§ұ `CampaignBootstrap` is now a **7-mode** director (hub вҮ„ dungeon вҮ„ Netheril вҮ„ Crown Wars вҮ„ Fugue вҮ„
  Vault вҮ„ encounter). 67 scripts / ~7.7k LOC, all clean.

---

## рҹ’° v0.8.3 вҖ” *"The Margin Pays Out"* вҖ” Vault Rewards (CODE)

> Solving the Lady's riddles now actually *rewards* you вҖ” narrative boons, not a +2 sword.

- рҹӘҷ **Coin of the Tenth Guest** (5 riddles solved) вҖ” a usable consumable that mends you with a *nudge
  of fate* (3d8 heal). *"Spend it when fate needs a nudge."*
- рҹҺҒ **Her Favour** (10 solved, high amusement) вҖ” a stronger single-use mending (6d8). *"Use it the
  moment you'd otherwise lose someone."*
- рҹ“ң **The Reader's Boon** (solve the secret 11th вҖ” her name) вҖ” a lore trophy + a flag the finale
  checks. *"Proof that, once, the margin smiled."*
- вҡҷпёҸ Rewards are granted **once per milestone** (flag-guarded) by `RiddleVaultUI`, dropped straight into
  the party pouch and usable from the inventory screen.

## рҹ§© v0.8.2 вҖ” *"The Vault Made Real"* вҖ” The Riddle Room, In Engine (CODE)

> The Lady in the Margins steps off the page: a playable riddle room built on the existing engine.

- рҹҺӯ **`RiddleContent`** вҖ” 15 symbolic **answer-tokens** (as quest items), the **10 object riddles**,
  the **brazier (spoken) riddles**, the locked *Your Name*, the secret 11th (*her* name), and **Tally's**
  hub dialogue.
- рҹҸӣпёҸ **`RiddleVault`** вҖ” the **Vault of Tens** as an explorable room: ten pedestals (place a token), a
  row of braziers (speak the word), the violet **Margin Brazier** (the twist riddle), and a way out;
  she hands you the pouch of tokens on entry.
- рҹ–ҘпёҸ **`RiddleVaultUI`** вҖ” solve riddles by **placing a token from the pouch** or **typing the spoken
  answer**; the **wit-beats-correctness** system rewards clever-wrong tokens with *amusement* instead of
  a solve, and failure costs only her interest вҖ” **she never kills you, she only gets bored.**
- рҹ”— Wired in: **Tally** appears in the Baldur's Gate hub; hearing her out (`vault.requested`) sends the
  director into the Vault (now a **6-mode** director). Plus **`RiddleVaultDemo`** for a one-click test.
- рҹ§ұ A small modal guard (`RiddleVaultUI.AnyOpen`) so clicking the puzzle panel doesn't also move your
  token. 64 scripts / ~7.1k LOC, all clean.

---

## рҹҺӯ v0.8.1 вҖ” *"The Note in the Margin"* вҖ” The Riddler & the Vault of Tens

> A surreal, chaotic-neutral fifth-dimensional entity who *monitors the situation* вҖ” and a riddle
> room better than Bodhi's, with twenty original riddles.

- рҹҺӯ **`22_THE_LADY_IN_THE_MARGINS.md`** вҖ” the recurring riddler in the lineage of **G-Man / the
  Outsider / Gaunter O'Dimm / Mr. Door**: chaotic neutral, beyond gender/comprehension, wants only to
  be *entertained.* Her **HUGE late twist** вҖ” she is the **ascended form of Naeve**, riddling you from
  the white space at the end of time (a character you've been interacting with all along,
  pre-ascension) вҖ” with a full foreshadowing ledger so it's *fair.*
- рҹ§© **The Vault of Tens** вҖ” a riddle room that keeps BG2's place-the-object joy and adds four things:
  **wit beats correctness** (clever-wrong answers are rewarded), **no death вҖ” only boredom**,
  **token combinations / cross-reference**, and **tiered narrative rewards** (a reroll, a truth, a
  witness вҖ” never a +2 sword).
- рҹ“ң **20 original D&D riddles** (+ the secret 21st = her name) вҖ” answers as **objects to place** or
  **words to speak**, several woven into the game's own themes (the MirrorвҶ’the Last Returned, the
  SkullвҶ’the Crown of Horns, *Your Name*вҶ’the master key, *Tomorrow*вҶ’the deathless Now, and *the Wall of
  the Faithless*, "the one she didn't write"). Includes implementation notes mapping the Vault onto the
  existing engine (pedestal Interactables + token items + flags).

---

## рҹӘһ v0.8.0 вҖ” *"Reflections & the First Sin"* вҖ” The Crown Wars, the Echoes, Tiled Floors & Aldric's Tea (CODE)

> A second era (proving the module pattern twice), the reflection-fight against yourself, a real
> isometric floor, and the marquee Act I conversation вҖ” all playable.

- рҹҢ«пёҸ **Crown Wars era** (`CrownWarsEra` + `CrownWarsContent`) вҖ” an elven high court ~10,000 years
  back, reached via a **second "Deep Skip" rift** after Netheril. Recruit **Ilfaeril**, and the
  signature **moral-hazard scene**: *The Verdict*, where you can **argue a soul-damnation down**
  with a skill check (proving the Wall was a *decision*) вҖ” shifting flags + Ilfaeril's approval.
- рҹӘһ **The Echoes / the Mirror fight** (`MirrorResolver`, `EncounterBuilder.mirrorMode`,
  `MirrorEncounterDemo`) вҖ” fight twisted **clones of your own party** (new `CharacterSheet.Clone()`)
  plus **the Last Returned**, who *kneels and yields* once its Echoes fall rather than dying by
  damage. The late-game centrepiece, in miniature.
- рҹҹ« **Tiled isometric floor** (`TileFloorRenderer`) вҖ” every scene now paints a checker-tinted
  diamond floor under the units (walls/voids drawn dark). A real visual upgrade, no art needed.
- вҳ• **"Tea with a Heretic"** (`AldricContent`) вҖ” Aldric's full branching conversation, in-engine;
  he comes to the Baldur's Gate hub once you've cleared the Cinderhaunt.
- рҹ§ұ `CampaignBootstrap` now drives a **5-mode** director (hub вҮ„ dungeon вҮ„ Netheril вҮ„ Crown Wars вҮ„
  encounter) and auto-recruits Naeve & Ilfaeril by flag. 60 scripts / ~6.6k LOC, all clean.

---

## рҹҢҶ v0.7.0 вҖ” *"The Falling City"* вҖ” Netheril, the First Time-Travel Era (CODE)

> The saga's time-travel becomes *playable.* You step through a rift in Baldur's Gate into a
> Netherese enclave falling out of the sky вҖ” and fight as the floor caves in beneath you.

- рҹ•°пёҸ **`NetherilEra`** вҖ” an explorable golden-rubble enclave (Karsus's Folly, вҲ’339 DR): arrive
  out of time (auto-played fall sequence), find **Naeve** in the rubble, recruit her, and trigger
  the battle. Flag-tracked like the Cinderhaunt so it survives the round-trip to combat.
- рҹ•іпёҸ **`FallingHazard`** вҖ” the era's signature mechanic: after a short grace period, the floor
  **collapses each turn from the edges inward** вҖ” voided tiles block movement and deal falling
  damage; it never collapses below a safe core, so the fight stays winnable but frantic.
  `EncounterBuilder` now has an `environmentalHazard` toggle.
- рҹ§ҷ **`NetherilContent`** вҖ” arcane abilities (Arcane Bolt, Lightning Lance, **Shatterglass** AoE,
  construct slams), the **Netherese War-Construct** roster, **Naeve** (Wizard companion), and the
  era arrival + recruit dialogue.
- рҹҢҖ **Rift transition** вҖ” after clearing the Cinderhaunt, a **Skip rift** appears in the hub;
  `CampaignBootstrap` now drives a 4-mode director (hub вҮ„ dungeon вҮ„ era вҮ„ encounter) and
  auto-recruits Naeve via dialogue flag, into the roster and into the falling-city fight.
- рҹҢҶ **`NetherilDemo`** вҖ” one-click jump straight into the collapsing-floor battle.
- рҹ“Ҳ 54 scripts / ~5.8k LOC, all brace-balanced and namespace-clean.

---

## рҹҗү v0.6.6 вҖ” *"Monsters, Money & Act One"* вҖ” Bestiary, Pitch & the Full Act I Script

> The combat-as-theme bestiary, the document that makes it fundable, and Act I scene by scene.

- рҹҗү **`19_BESTIARY_AND_BOSSES.md`** вҖ” enemies & bosses mapped to our combat engine: stat blocks,
  the **Lay vs. Shatter** mercy mechanic, the **Echoes** (mirror fights vs. your own party), and the
  **anti-bosses** (the Unmade and the Last Returned вҖ” beaten by *not* fighting). Every enemy is *a
  question with a health bar.*
- рҹҡҖ **`20_PITCH_AND_VERTICAL_SLICE.md`** вҖ” the Kickstarter-grade **pitch one-pager** (logline, 5 USPs,
  comparables) + the **one-hour vertical-slice spec** that proves the whole game + honest **scope,
  budget tiers, and risk**.
- рҹҺ¬ **`21_ACT_ONE_SCRIPT.md`** вҖ” the **full Act I script**, Prologue + 3 chapters, scene by scene
  (purpose В· beats В· branches В· flags), with an Act-I reactivity ledger feeding the later payoffs.

---

## рҹ’һ v0.6.5 вҖ” *"Hearts & Endings"* вҖ” Romances, Ending Prose & the Art/Music Bible

> The game gets a heart, a curtain call, and a face & a voice.

- рҹ’һ **`16_ROMANCE_SCRIPTS.md`** вҖ” full **romance arcs** for Garrow, Roen, Naeve, and Varra вҖ” six
  stages each (Spark вҶ’ Trust вҶ’ Turn вҶ’ Crisis вҶ’ Choosing вҶ’ The Last Night), with key-beat dialogue,
  approval gating, and how each romance becomes the finale's `anchor`. Each romance is an *argument
  about a theme* (faith / belonging / guilt / worth).
- рҹҢ„ **`17_ENDINGS_PROSE.md`** вҖ” all **six endings written as full prose epilogues** (+ the hidden
  "Husk" failure-state): the final scene, the per-companion slides, and the last image, each landing
  the cosmos on a single human face.
- рҹҺЁрҹҺј **`18_ART_AND_MUSIC_BIBLE.md`** вҖ” the **color language** (*warmth = mortality*), per-era and
  per-character visual identity (silhouette-first), UI/diegetic design, and a **leitmotif-driven
  score** built on one unfinished six-note phrase (*The Niche*) that finally resolves on your true
  name in the finale.

---

## рҹ§¬ v0.6.4 вҖ” *"Engineering the Gasp"* вҖ” Twist Architecture & Two Devastating Scenes

> The craft principles, baked into the structure вҖ” plus the two scenes designed to make players
> say *"HOLY SHIT."*

- рҹ§¬ **`13_TWIST_ARCHITECTURE.md`** вҖ” the redesign: a **Foreshadowing Ledger** (every clue вҶ’ its
  payoff, to pass the replay test), the **early permanent loss** design, the **weaponized-kindness**
  placement, **Mirror** visual staging, "**land the cosmos on one face**," the once-only
  **meta-crossing**, and a revised beat sheet sequencing all of it.
- рҹӘӨ **`14_SCENE_WEAPONIZED_KINDNESS.md`** вҖ” full scene: the reveal that the player's *compassion*
  (pulling Maerin from the Wall) is the loop's engine вҖ” *mercy as the trap.* Branching, shown-not-told.
- рҹ•іпёҸ **`15_SCENE_THE_BREACH.md`** вҖ” full scene: the game's first **irreversible loss**, with an
  **authored-fate system** (who the Wall takes depends on the player's earlier care). Teaches the
  player this story will take things and keep them.

---

## рҹҺ¬ v0.6.3 вҖ” *"Scenes & Craft"* вҖ” Dialogue Scripts, Side Quests & Emotional Design

> The set-piece conversations, the living city, and a craft study of the genre's greatest twists.

- рҹ’¬ **`10_DIALOGUE_SCRIPTS.md`** вҖ” full branching dialogue trees (node format, with checks/flags/
  approval) for the three marquee scenes: **"Tea with a Heretic"** (Aldric), **"The Offer"** (the
  Unmade at the Wall), and **"The Mirror"** (the Last Returned).
- рҹ—әпёҸ **`11_SIDEQUESTS_AND_NPCS.md`** вҖ” themed Baldur's Gate **side quests** (each a small echo of the
  central question), per-era side content, a roster of **memorable NPCs**, and **reactive world state**.
- рҹ’Ҙ **`12_EMOTIONAL_DESIGN.md`** вҖ” a craft study of the **20 most-remembered RPG moments** (Aerith,
  Revan, Planescape, Mordin, the Bloody Baron, Undertale, NieR, Spec OpsвҖҰ), the anatomy of a
  "HOLY SHIT" twist, and an **honest audit** of how *The Crown of Horns* reaches that tier.

---

## рҹ–ӢпёҸ v0.6.2 вҖ” *"Flesh and Bone"* вҖ” The Story, Fully Fleshed Out

> Everything deepened: full companion arcs, villain origin novellas, the esoteric texts, and
> prose treatments of the key scenes. ~12k more words of canon.

- рҹҺӯ **`06_COMPANIONS_DEEP.md`** вҖ” complete dossiers for all seven: full backstories, three-chapter
  **personal quests**, **romance arcs** beat-by-beat, cross-companion **banter**, approval triggers,
  and every fate. (Garrow, Roen, Varra, Naeve, Ilfaeril, Maerin, the Mournlight.)
- рҹ‘ҒпёҸ **`07_VILLAINS_DEEP.md`** вҖ” **origin novellas**: Aldric's forty years of graves; Myrkul's long
  patience; **the Unmade told from its own point of view**; the Last Returned's burned timeline;
  Vayle's terrible honesty; Jergal's boredom.
- рҹ“ң **`08_CODEX.md`** вҖ” the **esoteric texts in full** (*The Ledger of the Unwalled*, *Karsus's Last
  Theorem*, *The Ilfaeril Confession*, *The Doomsong of Jergal*, *The Niche*), factions, the
  time-travel **timeline**, the **bestiary**, and the **places**.
- вңҚпёҸ **`09_PROSE.md`** вҖ” novella-grade **prose treatments**: the Death, the Wall, the **Deathless
  Garden**, the **Mirror** (the duel with your future self), and the **Name** (the finale).
- рҹ”— Story library index updated.

## рҹ“ҡ v0.6.1 вҖ” *"The Deep Water"* вҖ” The Complete Story Bible

> A full, novel-grade narrative library вҖ” the story fleshed out to BG2 / Planescape depth.

- рҹ“– New **`docs/story/`** library (6 documents, ~30k words of canon):
  - `00_OVERVIEW` вҖ” tone, the central question, themes, and the **tropes we play & subvert**.
  - `01_SYNOPSIS` вҖ” the **entire game**, beginning to end, every twist in order.
  - `02_CHARACTERS` вҖ” deep backstories for the Returned, the **four villain masks**, Vayle, Jergal,
    and all **seven companions** (wound В· secret В· want vs. need В· arc В· personal quest В· romance В· fates).
  - `03_ACTS` вҖ” Prologue + five acts: settings, quests, set-pieces, the major development & twist of each.
  - `04_ENDINGS` вҖ” all **six endings** (+ a hidden failure-state) with flag requirements and per-companion
    epilogue slides.
  - `05_LORE_AND_PHILOSOPHY` вҖ” the cosmology, **esoteric in-world texts** (with quotes), the philosophical
    debates each faction embodies, and the recurring symbols.
- рҹ”— `STORY_BIBLE.md` and `README.md` now point into the deep library.

## рҹ•ҜпёҸ v0.6.0 вҖ” *"The Cinderhaunt"* вҖ” A Real Dungeon, Recruitment & the Time-Spanning Saga

> The world loop deepens into an actual dungeon crawl with a recruitable companion вҖ” and
> the story explodes into a time-travel epic across Realms history.

### рҹҸ° The Cinderhaunt Dungeon *(new)*
- рҹ—әпёҸ `Cinderhaunt`: a **two-chamber dungeon** beneath Baldur's Gate вҖ” outer harvest-hall and
  inner sanctum, split by an **iron door** that needs the **Cinderhaunt Key** (found in the
  hub strongbox).
- вҡ”пёҸ A **guard fight** and a **boss** (the Unbound Maw), triggered from the world; your whole
  **active party** (hero + Garrow + recruits) deploys into each battle.
- рҹ§  Progress is **flag-tracked** вҖ” cleared fights, the opened door, and looted chests all
  persist across the exploreвҶ”combat round-trips (new `lootFlag` on containers).
- рҹ§ұ `CampaignBootstrap` now drives a 3-mode director: **hub вҮ„ dungeon вҮ„ encounter**, with a
  forgiving "recover at the door" on a wipe.

### рҹ§‘вҖҚрҹӨқвҖҚрҹ§‘ Companion Recruitment *(new)*
- рҹӘ¶ **Roen Alleywind**, a Harper rogue, is recruitable in the hub via a branching conversation;
  a dialogue **flag** adds him to the roster and into combat. The director watches
  `companion.<id>.recruited` and recruits automatically вҖ” fully data-driven.

### рҹ“– The Story, Reborn *(major)*
- рҹҢҢ **`STORY_BIBLE.md` rewritten as a time-spanning, existential epic** (BG2 / Planescape
  scale): the **Unmade** (the accreted nothing of every dissolved Faithless soul), **time
  travel** through **Netheril (Karsus's Folly)**, the **Crown Wars**, the **Time of Troubles**,
  and the **Spellplague**; four nested villains ending in **the Last Returned** вҖ” your own
  future self; **7 companions across time**; **5 acts**; **6 endings**; and the twist that
  *you are the Unmade's origin.*

---

## рҹҺ’ v0.5.0 вҖ” *"Spoils & Spellfire"* вҖ” Loot, Equipment & the VFX Pipeline

> Gear up and light up: a full items/loot/equipment layer plus a combat **VFX system**
> that plays the supplied pixel-effect pack on hits and spells.

### рҹҺ’ Items, Loot & Equipment *(new)*
- рҹ—ғпёҸ `ItemDatabase` (id вҶ’ item registry) + content items (swords, armor, **Potion of
  Healing**, the Cinderhaunt Key).
- рҹӣЎпёҸ `EquipmentSystem` / `Equipment`: equip weapons & armor вҖ” gear drives **AC** and the
  basic attack; consumables apply effects on use.
- рҹҺ’ `InventoryScreen` (press **I**): backpack, gold, per-member equipped slots, equip/unequip/use.
- рҹ’° **Loot drops**: enemies drop gold + items, auto-awarded to the party on victory.
- рҹ“Ұ **Lootable containers**: a hub strongbox transfers its contents to the party stash.

### рҹ’Ҙ VFX & Asset Pipeline *(new)*
- вңЁ `FxSystem` + `FxAnimator`: fire-and-forget sprite-frame effects played on hit/cast,
  **auto-loaded** from `Resources/FX/<effect>/` (no inspector wiring; no-ops if absent).
- рҹ”Ҙ Abilities gained `hitVfx` / `castVfx`; impacts **auto-pick by damage type**
  (fire/ice/holy/вҖҰ). Healing plays a `heal` effect.
- рҹ“– New **`docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`**: exactly where to drop the pixel FX pack (and
  future character sprites, portraits, tilemaps) so they plug straight in.

---

## рҹ§ӯ v0.4.0 вҖ” *"The Gilded Gate"* вҖ” Exploration, the Hub & the World Loop

> The disconnected systems become an actual game: **explore a town, take a quest, walk
> into a dungeon, fight, and return** вҖ” the core Baldur's-Gate loop.

### рҹ§ӯ Exploration Mode *(new)*
- рҹ—әпёҸ `ExplorationController`: real-time **click-to-move** the party leader (A* pathing),
  plus **E**/click to interact; movement locks during conversations.
- рҹ§© `Interactable`: **NPCs** (talk), **exits/doors** (transition), **points of interest**
  (examine) вҖ” snaps to the grid and routes the party beside it.
- рҹ–ҘпёҸ `ExplorationHUD`: party vitals, an **interaction prompt**, examine flavor, and a
  **quest journal** whose objectives tick live from GameFlags.

### рҹҸ° Baldur's Gate Hub *(new)*
- рҹҸҷпёҸ `BaldursGateHub`: a walkable Lower City slice вҖ” the **Herald** (quest giver, branching
  convo), a **proclamation board** to examine, and the **Cinderhaunt stairs** to descend.

### рҹ”Ғ Mode Director & Reusable Combat *(new)*
- рҹҺ¬ `CampaignBootstrap`: the flagship entry вҖ” **create вҶ’ explore вҶ’ quest вҶ’ dungeon fight вҶ’
  XP/level вҶ’ return to the hub**, with persistent managers across modes.
- рҹ§ұ `EncounterBuilder`: drop-in turn-based encounter from a roster + victory callback, so
  **any door or trigger** can start a fight. (Combat HUD now tears down cleanly per mode.)

---

## рҹҸӣпёҸ v0.3.0 вҖ” *"What the Dead Owe"* вҖ” Setting, Creation, Leveling & the Playable Prologue

> The project moves to the **Forgotten Realms / Sword Coast** and gains a full
> create-a-hero вҶ’ dialogue вҶ’ battle вҶ’ level-up loop with a real uGUI HUD.

### рҹҢҚ Setting & Story
- рҹ—әпёҸ **Story Bible rewritten for the Forgotten Realms** (`docs/STORY_BIBLE.md`): the
  **Wall of the Faithless**, villain **Aldric Morn** & the **Crown of Horns** (Myrkul),
  **Sister Vayle**, **Jergal**, 7 FR companions, factions (Harpers, Flaming Fist, Order of
  the Gauntlet, Zhentarim, church of Kelemvor), 3 acts, and **five branching endings**.

### рҹ§ҷ Character Creation *(new)*
- рҹ§¬ `BackgroundDefinition` assets (skills, feature, **flag that unlocks dialogue**).
- рҹӣ пёҸ `CharacterBuilder`: **27-point point-buy** + **standard array**, racial bonuses,
  HP/AC assembly, background kit & flags, the **Returned** trait.
- рҹ–ҘпёҸ `CharacterCreationScreen`: race/class/background pickers + point-buy stepper.

### рҹ“Ҳ Leveling & XP *(new)*
- вӯҗ `Progression`: full **5e XP table** (1вҶ’20), HP & ability grants on level-up,
  proficiency scaling, `OnLevelUp` event.
- рҹҸҶ **XP awarded on victory** вҖ” pooled from defeated foes, split among survivors
  (`EncounterController`), can trigger level-ups mid-run.

### рҹ–ҘпёҸ Real uGUI HUD *(new)*
- рҹҺӣпёҸ `CombatHUD`: runtime-built canvas вҖ” **party portraits + live HP bars**, initiative,
  active-unit vitals/economy, a **clickable ability bar**, combat log, End Turn. Zero setup.
- рҹ—ЁпёҸ `DialogueScreen`: speaker/body/choices with live **skill-check** results; auto-play
  & on-finished hooks.

### рҹҸ° Act I Content Scaffold *(new)*
- рҹ“Ұ `SwordCoastContent`: builds FR **races, classes, backgrounds, spells/weapons, status
  effects**, the **opening dialogue** with Aldric's herald, and the **first quest** in code.
- рҹҺ¬ `PrologueBootstrap`: the flagship demo вҖ” **creation вҶ’ dialogue вҶ’ turn-based battle вҶ’
  XP/level вҶ’ quest completion**, fully self-contained.

### рҹ“ҡ Docs
- вңЁ New **`FEATURES.md`** (implemented + planned codex with status icons & badges).
- вңЁ **README** redesigned with badges, feature grid, and quick-start tables.

---

## вҡ”пёҸ v0.2.0 вҖ” Combat Depth Layer

> The systems that make combat *feel* like D&D 5e.

- вңЁ **Spell slots / resources** spent by leveled spells, refreshed at combat start.
- вҳ пёҸ **Status effects / conditions** (`StatusEffect.cs`, `Condition.cs`): duration, DoT,
  incapacitation, advantage grants, flat AC/attack/speed modifiers.
- вҡ–пёҸ **Advantage / disadvantage** in `AttackResolver` (cancel per 5e).
- рҹҺҜ **Saving-throw spells with save-for-half** and **healing abilities**.
- рҹ§© **`AbilityRunner`**: one validated entry point вҖ” range, slots, action economy, **AoE**,
  condition application, logging. Player input & enemy AI both use it.
- рҹӣЎпёҸ **Equipment hooks** on `CharacterSheet`.
- рҹ”Ҙ **Demo upgrade**: wizard (Firebolt + **Fireball**), cleric (**Healing Word**), and a
  poison-clawing enemy. HUD shows conditions, slots, and a numbered ability bar.

---

## рҹ§ұ v0.1.0 вҖ” Initial Starter

> The foundation.

- рҹ—әпёҸ Grid + isometric projection, **A\* pathfinding**, isometric camera.
- рҹҺІ Turn-based combat: initiative + action economy + win/loss.
- рҹ§ҷ 5e stats: abilities, modifiers, proficiency, AC, HP, d20 attacks vs AC.
- рҹ’¬ Data-driven **dialogue / quests / items** via ScriptableObjects.
- рҹ§  **GameFlags** story brain; рҹ’ҫ JSON **save/load**.
- рҹ•№пёҸ One-click **playable demo** + the full **story bible**.
